# Overview | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Compiled:** January 16, 2026 **Status:** Hytale is currently in Early Access **Official Reference:** [Hytale Modding Strategy and Statusarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2025/11/hytale-modding-strategy-and-status)

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation#important-notice)

Important Notice


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Hytale is currently in **Early Access**. This documentation is based on official Hytale sources and community testing.

**Key Points:**

*   Official tools are actively being developed and improved.
    
*   Official GitBook documentation is in progress by Hytale developers.
    
*   **Take frequent backups** - crashes can cause data loss.
    

> _"We're building Hytale with modding at its core. Most of what you see in the game can be changed, extended, or removed entirely."_ - Slikey (Technical Director)

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation#if-you-need-further-help-feel-free-to-join-my-discord-and-write-a-message-to-britakee)

if you need further help, feel free to join my [Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/gCRv62araB)
, and write a message to @Britakee

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation#quick-start-guides)

🚀 Quick Start Guides


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation#for-content-creators-no-coding)

For Content Creators (No Coding):

**Creating Asset Packs:**

1.  Start with [Hytale Modding Overview](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview)
    
2.  Follow [Getting Started with Packs](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/02-getting-started-with-packs)
    
3.  Learn [Adding a Block](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block)
    
4.  Explore [Block Animations](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations)
     and [Block State Changing](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing)
    

**Required Tools:**

*   **Blockbench** (for 3D models)
    
*   **Image editor** (for textures)
    
*   **Text editor** (for JSON files)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation#for-developers-java-programming)

For Developers (Java Programming):

**Creating Plugins:**

1.  Read [Hytale Modding Overview](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview)
    
2.  Clone the [Plugin Project Template](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template)
     - Start with a working project!
    
3.  Follow [Getting Started with Plugins](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/07-getting-started-with-plugins)
    
4.  Study [Example Command: Show Title](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/11-example-command-show-title)
    

**Required Tools:**

*   **IntelliJ IDEA**
    
*   **Java 25 JDK**
    
*   **Gradle** (included in template)
    

**Quick Start:**

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation#what-are-mods-in-hytale)

What Are Mods in Hytale?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation#four-official-modding-categories)

Four Official Modding Categories:

1.  **Server Plugins (Java .jar files)**
    

*   **Purpose:** Extend server functionality programmatically.
    
*   **Use Cases:** Minigames, economies, custom logic.
    
*   **Tools:** Java 25, IntelliJ IDEA.
    

1.  **Data Assets (JSON files)**
    

*   **Purpose:** Drive gameplay behavior and define core content.
    
*   **Content:** Blocks, items, NPCs, world generation.
    
*   **Tools:** Asset Editor (no coding required).
    

1.  **Art Assets (Sounds, Models, Textures)**
    

*   **Purpose:** Visual and audio representation.
    
*   **Tools:** Blockbench (Official Support).
    

1.  **Save Files (Worlds and Prefabs)**
    

*   **Purpose:** Share complete creations and structures.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation#file-paths-quick-reference)

📂 File Paths Quick Reference


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**For Packs:** `%AppData%/Roaming/Hytale/UserData/mods/`

**For Plugins:** `%AppData%/Roaming/Hytale/UserData/earlyplugins/`

# Frequently Asked Questions | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Last Modified:** Friday, January 16, 2026

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#overview)

Overview


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This page answers frequently asked questions about Hytale modding, server architecture, and technical capabilities.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#client-and-server-architecture)

Client & Server Architecture


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#id-1.-can-the-client-be-modded)

1\. Can the client be modded?

**No**, the client cannot be modded directly.

**However:**

*   The server controls how the game and UI looks
    
*   Works similar to "Resource Packs" in Minecraft
    
*   The server decides what mods are used
    
*   Visuals are server-side controlled
    
*   No client-side mods needed for security and consistency
    

**Benefits of Server-Side Modding:**

*   Join any modded server without downloading external mods
    
*   One stable client for all players
    
*   Better security (no client modifications)
    
*   Unified community experience
    
*   Server owners control the experience
    

**Philosophy:**

> _"One Community, One Client"_ - Hytale avoids the fragmented ecosystem of different modded clients by keeping all modifications server-side.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#network-and-technical)

Network & Technical


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#id-2.-what-network-protocol-will-be-used)

2\. What Network Protocol will be used?

**Hytale uses the QUIC transport protocol.**

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#understanding-internet-protocols)

Understanding Internet Protocols:

**UDP (User Datagram Protocol):**

*   Connectionless and fast
    
*   Fire-and-forget packets
    
*   Less reliability (packets can be lost)
    

**TCP (Transmission Control Protocol):**

*   Connection-based
    
*   Slower than UDP
    
*   Guaranteed packet delivery
    
*   Much more reliability
    

**QUIC (Quick UDP Internet Connections):**

*   **Hybrid protocol** building on UDP
    
*   Same speed benefits as UDP
    
*   Adds reliability layers like TCP
    
*   **Excellent for game development**
    
*   Blends speed and reliability
    

**Why QUIC?**

*   Best of both worlds for multiplayer gaming
    
*   Modern, efficient protocol
    
*   Designed for low-latency applications
    
*   Industry-proven (used by Google, YouTube, etc.)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#server-infrastructure)

Server Infrastructure


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#id-3.-what-are-transfer-packets)

3\. What are Transfer Packets?

**Transfer packets** are small data payloads (4KB) that allow players to move from one server to another while carrying information.

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#key-points)

Key Points:

**What They Are:**

*   Small data containers (4KB limit)
    
*   Carry player information between servers
    
*   Enable seamless server transitions
    
*   Preserve inventory, stats, and progress
    

**What They Are NOT:**

*   **Not equivalent to BungeeCord or Velocity**
    
*   Do not manage network-wide features
    
*   Do not support global plugins
    
*   DDOS protection would be very difficult for small networks
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#best-use-cases)

Best Use Cases:

**Perfect For:**

*   Small server networks
    
*   Hub-based setups
    
*   Server-to-server player transfers
    
*   Preserving player state across servers
    

**Example Scenario:**

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#benefits)

Benefits:

*   **Lower Server Costs** - Distribute players across multiple servers
    
*   **Better Performance** - Dedicated servers for specific game modes
    
*   **Development Focus** - Less time on network infrastructure, more on gameplay
    
*   **Seamless Experience** - Players don't lose progress when switching servers
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#limitations)

Limitations:

*   Primarily intended for **smaller servers**
    
*   Not a full proxy solution like BungeeCord
    
*   4KB data limit per transfer
    
*   Network-wide features require custom implementation
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#id-4.-will-hytale-support-dedicated-servers)

4\. Will Hytale support dedicated servers?

**Yes!** Hytale will fully support dedicated servers.

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#what-this-means)

What This Means:

**Hosting Options:**

*   Host on your own hardware
    
*   Use third-party hosting services
    
*   Full control over server settings
    
*   Install and configure mods
    
*   Optimize performance
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#benefits-of-dedicated-servers)

Benefits of Dedicated Servers:

**Complete Control:**

*   Server settings and configurations
    
*   Mod installation and management
    
*   Performance tuning and optimization
    
*   Backup and maintenance schedules
    

**Flexibility:**

*   Choose your hosting provider
    
*   Scale resources as needed
    
*   Run custom plugins and packs
    
*   Full administrative access
    

**Professional Options:**

*   Enterprise-grade hosting
    
*   Custom hardware configurations
    
*   Advanced networking setups
    
*   Professional support options
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#hosting-methods)

Hosting Methods:

1.  **Self-Hosted** - Run on your own hardware
    
2.  **VPS/Cloud** - Rent virtual private servers (DigitalOcean, AWS, etc.)
    
3.  **Game Hosting** - Specialized game server hosts
    
4.  **Hybrid** - Mix of self-hosted and cloud resources
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#platform-support)

Platform Support


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#id-5.-will-hytale-support-modding-on-consoles)

5\. Will Hytale support modding on consoles?

**As of now, Hytale modding is primarily focused on PC platforms.**

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#current-status)

Current Status:

**PC Platforms:**

*   Windows
    
*   macOS
    
*   Linux
    

**Console Support:**

*   Not confirmed for modding
    
*   Game may come to consoles in the future
    
*   Modding tools designed for PC
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#why-pc-first)

Why PC-First?

**Technical Reasons:**

*   Modding requires file system access
    
*   Console platforms have restrictions
    
*   Development tools are PC-based
    
*   Testing and iteration easier on PC
    

**Platform Limitations:**

*   Console manufacturers restrict modifications
    
*   Certification processes are complex
    
*   Updates and patches have approval delays
    
*   File access is limited or prohibited
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#future-possibilities)

Future Possibilities:

While current modding support is PC-focused, the team hasn't ruled out future console support for:

*   Playing on modded servers (server-side mods)
    
*   Official mod marketplace
    
*   Curated content packs
    

**Stay Updated:**

*   Follow official Hytale announcements
    
*   Join the [Official Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/hytale)
    
*   Check the [Hytale Blogarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-frequently-asked-questions#getting-help)

Getting Help


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Official Channels:**

*   **Discord:** [Official Hytale Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/hytale)
    
*   **Blog:** [Hytale Newsarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news)

# Youtube Tutorials | Hytale Modding Documentation

This tutorial by **Britakee** provides a step-by-step guide on using the in-game Asset Editor to create your first Pack and add a custom item to Hytale.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-youtube-tutorials#hytale-modding-tutorial-1-setup-packs-and-custom-item)

Hytale Modding Tutorial #1: Setup Packs & Custom Item


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> **Note:** If the video player above does not appear, you can [click here to watch on YouTubearrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_XwdR1fOl5U)
> .

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-youtube-tutorials#key-takeaways)

Key Takeaways


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Asset Editor Access:** To use the editor, you must first op yourself in a creative world by typing `/op self` in the chat \[[00:56arrow-up-right](http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_XwdR1fOl5U&t=56)\
    \].
    
*   **Pack Creation:** Packs can be created directly within the Asset Editor by clicking the three dots in the corner and selecting "Add Pack" \[[01:18arrow-up-right](http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_XwdR1fOl5U&t=78)\
    \].
    
*   **Folder Setup:** After creating a pack in-game, you must manually create a `Common/Resources` folder structure in the pack's directory to hold your texture files \[[02:10arrow-up-right](http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_XwdR1fOl5U&t=130)\
    \].
    
*   **Custom Items:** You can quickly create new items by using the "Copy Asset" feature to duplicate an existing Hytale item and then modifying its texture and properties \[[02:52arrow-up-right](http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_XwdR1fOl5U&t=172)\
    \].
    
*   **Localization:** To fix the item's name in the inventory, you need to create a `Server/Languages/en-US/server.lang` file and define the item name key \[[04:05arrow-up-right](http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_XwdR1fOl5U&t=245)\
    \].
    
*   **Sharing Mods:** To make your mod available globally, compress the manifest and folders into a `.zip` file and move it to `%AppData%/Hytale/UserData/Mods/` \[[04:52arrow-up-right](http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_XwdR1fOl5U&t=292)\
    \].
    

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-youtube-tutorials#getting-help)

Getting Help


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Official Channels:**

*   **Discord:** [Official Hytale Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/hytale)
    
*   **Blog:** [Hytale Newsarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news)
    

[PreviousTechnical Insightschevron-left](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights)
[NextHytale Modding Overviewchevron-right](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview)

Last updated 1 day ago

*   [Key Takeaways](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-youtube-tutorials#key-takeaways)

# Hytale Modding Overview | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [Official Hytale Modding Strategyarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2025/11/hytale-modding-strategy-and-status)

**Last Modified:** Friday, January 10, 2026

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#introduction)

Introduction


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Welcome to Hytale modding! This documentation provides comprehensive tutorials and guides for creating mods in Hytale, from asset packs to advanced Java plugins.

> **Important:** Hytale is currently in **Early Access**. The modding tools and documentation are actively being developed and improved. Expect rough edges, but also expect rapid improvements based on community feedback.

> **Official Statement:** _"We're building Hytale with modding at its core. Most of what you see in the game can be changed, extended, or removed entirely."_ - Slikey (Technical Director)

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#four-official-modding-categories)

Four Official Modding Categories


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

According to Hytale's official modding strategy, Hytale modding falls into **four technical categories**:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#id-1.-server-plugins-java-.jar-files)

1\. Server Plugins (Java .jar files)

**Server Plugins** are Java-based mods that:

*   Extend the functionality of the server programmatically
    
*   Are extremely powerful and allow deep modifications to gameplay and core systems
    
*   Enable you to build minigames, economies, commands, custom logic, new asset types, and more
    
*   Require Java programming knowledge
    

**Use Cases:**

*   Custom game modes and minigames
    
*   Economy systems
    
*   Custom commands
    
*   Server management tools
    
*   Advanced gameplay mechanics
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#id-2.-data-assets-json-files)

2\. Data Assets (JSON files)

**Data Assets** drive gameplay behavior and define core content:

*   **Blocks and Items** - Define properties, behaviors, and interactions
    
*   **NPCs** - Configure mob behavior and AI
    
*   **World Generation** - Control terrain, biomes, and structures
    
*   **Drop Tables and Loot** - Define what items drop from blocks and mobs
    
*   **And more** - Most game content is data-driven
    

**Key Feature:** No coding required - edit JSON files to modify game content

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#id-3.-art-assets-sounds-models-textures)

3\. Art Assets (Sounds, Models, Textures)

**Art Assets** provide the visual and audio representation of game elements:

*   **Models** - 3D block and entity models
    
*   **Textures** - Visual appearance of blocks, items, and entities
    
*   **Sounds** - Audio effects and music
    
*   **Animations** - Movement and behavior animations
    

**Official Tool:** Blockbench is officially supported for creating Hytale models, textures, and animations

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#id-4.-save-files-worlds-and-prefabs)

4\. Save Files (Worlds and Prefabs)

**Save Files** allow you to share complete creations:

*   **Worlds** - Share entire playable worlds
    
*   **Prefabs** - Prebuilt structures like trees, houses, or landmarks
    
*   **Usage** - Prefabs are used in creative tools and world generation
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#important-no-text-based-scripting)

Important: No Text-Based Scripting


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Official Clarification:** Hytale will **NOT** support text-based scripting languages like Lua.

**Why?**

*   Text-based scripting claims to "help non-programmers" but still requires programming concepts
    
*   It forces programmers to juggle two languages
    
*   It increases complexity for both designers and programmers
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#instead-visual-scripting-coming-soon)

Instead: Visual Scripting (Coming Soon)

Hytale will implement **Visual Scripting** (similar to Unreal Engine Blueprints):

*   **For Designers:** Build logic visually without coding
    
*   **For Programmers:** Extend the system by creating new nodes in Java
    
*   **Sandboxed and Safe:** Visual scripts can be shared safely without security risks
    
*   **Future Vision:** Visual scripting directly in the 3D world (link levers, doors, triggers, etc.)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#modding-philosophy)

Modding Philosophy


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Hytale's modding is built on key principles:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#server-side-first)

Server-Side First

*   All modding is server-based (both singleplayer and multiplayer)
    
*   Join any modded server without downloading external mods
    
*   No client-side mods for security and consistency
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#one-community-one-client)

One Community, One Client

*   Avoid fragmented ecosystem with different modded clients
    
*   Client remains stable, secure, and consistent
    
*   Servers provide creativity and variation
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#modding-for-longevity)

Modding for Longevity

*   Long-term commitment to modding support
    
*   Built with the same tools used to create the game
    
*   "Anything we do, you can do as well"
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#official-modding-tools)

Official Modding Tools


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Hytale provides several official tools for creating content:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#id-1.-hytale-asset-editor)

1\. Hytale Asset Editor

*   **Purpose:** Editor for data assets (JSON files)
    
*   **Status:** Available now
    
*   **Capabilities:** Supports most asset types
    
*   **Limitations:** Notable limitations around NPCs, world generation, and interactions (being improved)
    
*   **Access:** Built into the game
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#id-2.-blockbench-plugin)

2\. Blockbench Plugin

*   **Purpose:** Create Hytale-compatible models, textures, and animations
    
*   **Status:** Releasing soon
    
*   **Integration:** Direct integration with Blockbench
    
*   **Replaces:** Hytale's own internal modeling tools
    
*   **Why:** Better support for established creative workflows in the community
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#id-3.-asset-graph-editor)

3\. Asset Graph Editor

*   **Purpose:** Node-based editor for complex assets
    
*   **Status:** Currently being released
    
*   **Use Cases:** World generation, creative tool brushes, NPCs
    
*   **Note:** Internal tool being made public - expect rough edges but useful functionality
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#id-4.-creative-mode-tools)

4\. Creative Mode Tools

*   **Purpose:** Interactive suite of in-game world editing and creation tools
    
*   **Status:** Available in Early Access
    
*   **Access:** Switch to Creative Mode in any world
    
*   **Official Info:** [Creative Mode Blogarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2025/11/hytale-creative-mode)
    

**Available Tools:**

*   **Scripted Brushes** - Create mountains, paths, procedural ruins (asset-defined, modder-creatable)
    
*   **Shape Brush** - Paint pyramids, cones, squares with customizable size, density, materials
    
*   **Selection Tool** - 3D selections, copy, paste, move, rotate, save prefabs, regenerate chunks
    
*   **Paste Tool** - Precise prefab placement with arrow key controls
    
*   **Ruler/Laser Pointer** - Measure distances and point out locations
    
*   **Prefab Browser/Editor** - Browse 100+ models, edit in separate environment
    
*   **Player Model Changer** - Become any NPC model
    
*   **Machinima Camera** - Keyframe animation for cinematic recording
    

**Creative Mode Features:**

*   Customizable flight (speed, controls, hover/directional, inertia)
    
*   Quick Settings Panel (changes based on tool in hand)
    
*   Help Menu for quick command discovery
    
*   Real-time world modification with instant feedback
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#id-5.-machinima-tools)

5\. Machinima Tools

*   **Purpose:** Create cinematic content (used for the 2018 trailer)
    
*   **Status:** Available but needs technical fixes
    
*   **Quality:** Delivered great results for official trailers
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#id-6.-custom-ui-framework-noesisgui)

6\. Custom UI Framework (NoesisGUI)

*   **Purpose:** Create custom user interfaces
    
*   **Status:** In transition - consolidating from 3 UI frameworks to 1
    
*   **Framework:** NoesisGUI (official UI framework)
    
*   **Current State:** Asset-driven UIs are available but incomplete
    
*   **Recommendation:** Start experimenting and provide feedback
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#official-documentation-and-resources)

Official Documentation & Resources


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#official-hytale-documentation-gitbook)

Official Hytale Documentation (GitBook)

*   **Status:** In progress
    
*   **Platform:** GitBook (same as this documentation!)
    
*   **Note:** Will start incomplete but expand based on community questions
    
*   **Official Statement:** _"We are working on public creator documentation hosted on GitBook"_
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#server-source-code-coming-soon)

Server Source Code (Coming Soon)

*   **Release:** Within 1-2 months after Early Access launch (March 2026)
    
*   **Access:** Full server source code will be shared
    
*   **Purpose:** - Inspect how systems work under the hood
    
*   Unblock yourself when documentation is incomplete
    
*   Contribute improvements and bug fixes
    
*   **Note:** Server is not obfuscated - can be decompiled now
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#development-bounties-future)

Development Bounties (Future)

*   **Plan:** Open bounties for specific improvements and features
    
*   **Goal:** Reward contributions that strengthen the ecosystem
    
*   **Timeline:** Takes time to set up properly
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#community-and-support)

Community & Support


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#official-channels)

Official Channels

*   **Discord:** [Official Hytale Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/hytale)
     - Talk directly with developers and modders
    
*   **Discord (CurseForge):** [CurseForge UGC Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/S3EaZArYz2)
     - User-generated content focus
    
*   **X / Reddit:** Tweet at @Hytale or post on Hytale subreddits
    
*   **Official Blog:** [Hytale Newsarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news)
     - Latest updates and strategy posts
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#what-to-expect)

What to Expect

*   **Early Access Reality:** Tools are uneven, documentation is incomplete, some workflows are frustrating
    
*   **Rapid Improvements:** Developers are fixing issues as they come in
    
*   **Transparency:** Developers commit to being honest about what's ready and what's not
    
*   **Your Feedback Matters:** Hold developers accountable, demand answers, provide feedback
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#important-warnings)

Important Warnings


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#data-safety)

Data Safety

> **Critical:** Hytale is in true Early Access. There are crashes, and some can cause **data loss**.

**Practical Advice:**

*   **Take frequent backups** of your savegames and creations
    
*   Treat this phase as valuable but **not yet safe for irreplaceable work**
    
*   Automatic backup solutions are being developed
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#current-limitations)

Current Limitations

*   Missing editing capabilities for some features
    
*   Client behavior not fully exposed to server
    
*   Some tools are rough, inconsistent, or painful to work with
    
*   Modding maturity varies wildly depending on what you're building
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#long-term-vision)

Long-Term Vision


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#node-editors-coming)

Node Editors (Coming)

*   **Purpose:** Visual editors for complex JSON assets
    
*   **Target:** NPCs, Interactions, World Generation
    
*   **Integration:** Directly into Hytale Asset Editor
    
*   **Goal:** Unified creator suite instead of patchwork tools
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#visual-scripting-core-pillar)

Visual Scripting (Core Pillar)

*   **Timeline:** Long-term priority
    
*   **Features:**
    
*   Sandboxed, safe environment for sharing logic
    
*   Great learnability for all skill levels
    
*   Programmers can extend with performance-critical nodes
    
*   Eventually: Visual scripting directly in the 3D world
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#first-party-server-network)

First-Party Server Network

*   **Plan:** Hypixel-style minigames network
    
*   **Purpose:** - Validate modding tools at scale
    
*   Share code and assets for learning
    
*   Ensure playable content during early days
    
*   **Note:** Not trying to compete with community servers
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#getting-started)

Getting Started


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#for-content-creators-no-coding)

For Content Creators (No Coding)

1.  Start with **Packs** - Create blocks, items, and content using JSON
    
2.  Use the **Asset Editor** to modify properties visually
    
3.  Learn **Blockbench** for custom models and textures
    
4.  Follow the [Getting Started with Packs](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/02-getting-started-with-packs)
     guide
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#for-developers-java)

For Developers (Java)

1.  Learn **Java programming** fundamentals
    
2.  Set up your development environment (IntelliJ IDEA recommended)
    
3.  Clone the [Plugin Templatearrow-up-right](https://github.com/realBritakee/hytale-template-plugin)
    
4.  Follow the [Getting Started with Plugins](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/07-getting-started-with-plugins)
     guide
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#for-advanced-users)

For Advanced Users

1.  Explore **Bootstrap/Early Plugins** for low-level modifications
    
2.  Study the decompiled server source (or wait for official release)
    
3.  Follow the [Bootstrap/Early Plugins](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/09-bootstrap-early-plugins)
     guide
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#closing-words)

Closing Words


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

_From Slikey (Technical Director):_

> "If you're willing to join us in this phase - bugs, rough edges and all - you won't just be modding Hytale. You'll be shaping what Hytale modding becomes."

This documentation aims to help you navigate the current state of Hytale modding while preparing you for the exciting future ahead.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview#getting-help)

Getting Help


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Discord:** [Official Hytale Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/hytale)
    
*   **Blog:** [Hytale Newsarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news)

# Technical Insights | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Last Modified:** Friday, January 16, 2026

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Comprehensive summary of technical insights from Hytale developers covering architecture, modding, gameplay systems, and development philosophy.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#technical-architecture)

Technical Architecture


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#network-and-infrastructure)

Network & Infrastructure

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#what-network-protocol-does-hytale-use)

What network protocol does Hytale use?

**QUIC (Quick UDP Internet Connections)**

Hytale uses QUIC, which is a reliable UDP protocol with unreliable channels, instead of traditional TCP.

**Benefits:**

*   Fast like UDP
    
*   Reliable like TCP
    
*   Optimized for gaming
    
*   Modern internet standard
    

**Known Limitation:**

*   QUIC may be blocked in some regions
    
*   No alternative protocol currently planned
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#what-platforms-can-run-hytale-servers)

What platforms can run Hytale servers?

**Any platform supporting Java 25**

*   Windows (primary)
    
*   Linux (actively supported)
    
*   macOS (in development)
    
*   Any OS with Java 25 runtime
    

**Server Hosting:**

*   Available on day 1 of Early Access
    
*   No business agreements required
    
*   Just comply with EULA/TOS
    
*   Full self-hosting support
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#how-does-multiplayer-connectivity-work)

How does multiplayer connectivity work?

**Connection Methods:**

*   **Launch:** Direct IP connection
    
*   **Post-Launch:** Server discovery system planned
    
*   **No Authentication Server Required:** For direct connections
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#what-is-the-server-tick-rate)

What is the server tick rate?

**Default: 30 TPS (Ticks Per Second)**

*   Base server tick rate is 30 TPS
    
*   Can be changed using server plugins
    
*   Multi-core support for better performance
    
*   Each world has main thread + parallel execution
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#what-rendering-technology-does-hytale-use)

What rendering technology does Hytale use?

**OpenGL 3.3**

**Why OpenGL 3.3:**

*   Mac compatibility
    
*   Wide hardware support
    
*   Stable and proven
    

**Future Plans:**

*   Potential migration to Vulkan
    
*   Potential migration to Metal
    
*   Performance improvements planned
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#security-and-distribution)

Security & Distribution

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#can-clients-execute-custom-code)

Can clients execute custom code?

**No - Absolutely not.**

**Security Model:**

*   No client-side code execution
    
*   Prevents remote code execution exploits
    
*   Server controls everything
    
*   Safe, sandboxed environment
    

**What Clients Can Download:**

*   Configuration files
    
*   Assets (models, textures, sounds)
    
*   Executable code
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#how-are-mods-distributed)

How are mods distributed?

**Community Platforms**

**Primary Channels:**

*   [CurseForgearrow-up-right](https://www.curseforge.com/)
    
*   [Modrintharrow-up-right](https://modrinth.com/)
    
*   GitHub releases
    
*   Community websites
    

**In-Game Marketplace:**

*   Not planned for immediate launch
    
*   May be added later
    
*   Focus on community platforms first
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#modding-capabilities)

Modding Capabilities


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#server-side-power)

Server-Side Power

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#what-can-java-plugins-do)

What can Java plugins do?

**Full Java Access - Anything Java Can Do**

**Capabilities:**

*   Database connections (MySQL, PostgreSQL, MongoDB)
    
*   Web requests (REST APIs, webhooks)
    
*   Any Java library or framework
    
*   Custom systems (economy, permissions, clans)
    
*   Machine learning frameworks
    
*   Scripting languages (Lua, JavaScript)
    

**Example Use Cases:**

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#can-server-code-be-modified)

Can server code be modified?

**Yes - Full Server Source Access**

**Features:**

*   Shared server source code
    
*   Developer comments included
    
*   Unobfuscated code
    
*   Heavy modifications possible
    
*   Learn from official implementation
    

**Benefits:**

*   Understand how systems work
    
*   Unblock yourself when documentation is sparse
    
*   Contribute improvements and bug fixes
    
*   Create deep integrations
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#is-hot-reload-supported)

Is hot reload supported?

**Yes - For Most Asset Types**

**Hot Reload Support:**

*   JSON data files
    
*   Models and textures
    
*   World generation assets
    
*   Most visual assets
    
*   Some code changes may require restart
    

**Developer Experience:**

*   Fast iteration cycles
    
*   See changes immediately
    
*   No full server restarts needed
    
*   Efficient testing workflow
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#content-creation-no-code-required)

Content Creation (No Code Required)

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#can-i-create-custom-biomes-without-coding)

Can I create custom biomes without coding?

**Yes - Visual Node Editor**

**World Generation V2:**

*   Visual node-based editor
    
*   Custom biomes and maps
    
*   Terrain shape control
    
*   Prop placement systems
    
*   Material providers
    
*   Live-reload in-game
    

**No Java Knowledge Required:**

*   Accessible with tutorials and practice
    
*   Same tools used by Hytale team
    
*   Link simple nodes to create complex systems
    

See: [World Generation Modding](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#how-are-npcs-and-items-configured)

How are NPCs and items configured?

**JSON-Based Configuration**

**Data-Driven Systems:**

*   Items and blocks
    
*   NPC behavior and AI
    
*   Combat abilities
    
*   Loot tables
    
*   Crafting recipes
    
*   Custom interactions
    

**Hytale Asset Editor:**

*   Visual editor for JSON files
    
*   No coding required
    
*   Live preview of changes
    
*   Built into the game
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#what-is-visual-scripting)

What is Visual Scripting?

**Replaces Command Blocks**

**Features:**

*   Node-based logic builder
    
*   Fully sandboxed and safe
    
*   No coding required
    
*   Programmers can extend with custom nodes
    
*   Eventually: Visual scripting in 3D world
    

**Use Cases:**

*   Door mechanisms
    
*   Puzzle logic
    
*   Custom interactions
    
*   Quest triggers
    
*   Minigame mechanics
    

**Timeline:** Long-term priority, core pillar of Hytale modding

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#what-is-the-prefab-system)

What is the Prefab System?

**Sophisticated Building Blocks**

**Features:**

*   Prebuilt structures
    
*   In-game prefab editor
    
*   Trees, houses, landmarks
    
*   Creative tool integration
    
*   World generation usage
    

**Creator Tools:**

*   Browse 100+ official prefabs
    
*   Edit in separate environment
    
*   Save custom prefabs
    
*   Share with community
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#advanced-modding)

Advanced Modding

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#how-does-the-combat-system-work)

How does the combat system work?

**Data-Driven Interaction System**

**Features:**

*   Attack chains and combos
    
*   Custom abilities
    
*   Interaction sequences
    
*   Configurable via JSON
    
*   No coding required for basic combat
    

**Extensibility:**

*   Custom attack patterns
    
*   Unique weapon behaviors
    
*   Special abilities
    
*   Boss mechanics
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#are-there-sub-hitboxes-for-bosses)

Are there sub-hitboxes for bosses?

**Yes - But Needs Improvement**

**Current Status:**

*   Sub-hitbox support exists
    
*   Enables complex boss mechanics
    
*   System needs improvement
    
*   Actively being enhanced
    

**Use Cases:**

*   Multi-part bosses
    
*   Weak point targeting
    
*   Limb-specific damage
    
*   Complex enemy designs
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#can-i-create-custom-status-effects)

Can I create custom status effects?

**Yes - Buff/Debuff System**

**Features:**

*   Custom buffs and debuffs
    
*   Custom stats and attributes
    
*   Duration and stacking
    
*   Visual effects
    
*   Fully extensible
    

**Examples:**

*   Poison damage over time
    
*   Speed boosts
    
*   Armor buffs
    
*   Custom attribute modifiers
    
*   Unique effects
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#can-i-create-custom-uis)

Can I create custom UIs?

**Yes - NoesisGUI Transition**

**Current Status:**

*   Transitioning to NoesisGUI
    
*   Powerful interface customization
    
*   Asset-driven UIs available
    
*   Currently incomplete
    
*   Actively being improved
    

**Capabilities:**

*   Custom menus and HUDs
    
*   Interactive interfaces
    
*   Data visualization
    
*   Mini-map systems
    
*   Quest trackers
    

**Recommendation:** Start experimenting and provide feedback

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#how-does-block-physics-work)

How does block physics work?

**Selective System**

**What Falls:**

*   Trees collapse when chopped
    
*   Natural blocks can fall
    
*   Specific physics-enabled blocks
    

**What Doesn't Fall:**

*   Player-placed blocks (by default)
    
*   Buildings can float
    
*   Most constructed structures
    

**Why Selective:**

*   Gameplay balance
    
*   Building freedom
    
*   Performance considerations
    
*   Can be modded for different behavior
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#gameplay-systems)

Gameplay Systems


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#core-mechanics)

Core Mechanics

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#is-there-a-hunger-stamina-system)

Is there a hunger/stamina system?

**No Hunger by Default**

**Stamina System:**

*   Stamina for actions
    
*   No hunger mechanic
    
*   Can be modded in
    

**Design Philosophy:**

*   Focus on exploration and combat
    
*   Reduce survival tedium
    
*   Fully customizable by servers
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#how-does-gravity-work)

How does gravity work?

**Selective Block Physics**

**Natural Blocks:**

*   Trees fall when cut
    
*   Leaves decay
    
*   Sand/gravel may fall
    

**Player Structures:**

*   Buildings can float
    
*   No structural integrity requirements
    
*   Creative freedom prioritized
    

**Modding:**

*   Physics can be customized
    
*   Different rules for different blocks
    
*   Full control via plugins
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#whats-planned-for-lighting)

What's planned for lighting?

**Major Overhaul Planned**

**Current Issues:**

*   Model/voxel lighting inconsistencies
    
*   Some visual artifacts
    

**Improvements Coming:**

*   Fix model/voxel conflicts
    
*   Better light propagation
    
*   Enhanced shadow quality
    
*   More realistic lighting
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#what-is-the-world-height-limit)

What is the world height limit?

**Currently Limited**

**Status:**

*   Current height limit exists
    
*   May change with voxel storage updates
    
*   Technical limitations being addressed
    

**Future:**

*   Potential height increase
    
*   Voxel storage improvements
    
*   Better vertical world space
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#is-there-a-redstone-equivalent)

Is there a redstone equivalent?

**Not at Launch**

**Visual Scripting Instead:**

*   Node-based logic
    
*   More powerful than redstone
    
*   Sandboxed and safe
    
*   Fully moddable
    

**Can Be Modded:**

*   Plugins can add redstone-like systems
    
*   Community may create alternatives
    
*   Full flexibility for servers
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#player-systems)

Player Systems

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#what-character-models-are-available)

What character models are available?

**Humans by Default**

**Creative Mode:**

*   Change to any NPC model
    
*   Player Model Changer tool
    
*   Become any creature
    

**Multiplayer:**

*   Server-controlled avatars
    
*   No custom models in multiplayer (for now)
    
*   Skin customization available
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#can-i-customize-my-skin)

Can I customize my skin?

**Full Customization Possible**

> _"Mod yourself into a potato"_ - Developers

**Features:**

*   Complete skin customization
    
*   Upload custom textures
    
*   Unique character appearance
    
*   Creative freedom
    

**Cosmetics:**

*   Official cosmetic packs (low price)
    
*   Support server infrastructure
    
*   No pay-to-win
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#are-there-transformation-shapeshifting-mechanics)

Are there transformation/shapeshifting mechanics?

**Yes - Transformation Potions**

**Features:**

*   Potions that change player form
    
*   Transform into different creatures
    
*   Fun gameplay mechanic
    
*   Moddable for custom transformations
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#world-and-npcs)

World & NPCs

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#how-does-the-faction-system-work)

How does the faction system work?

**Living World with Dynamic NPCs**

**Features:**

*   Factions interact with each other
    
*   Dynamic relationships
    
*   Territory control
    
*   Player reputation
    
*   Consequence-driven world
    

**Immersion:**

*   NPCs remember player actions
    
*   World reacts to player choices
    
*   Ongoing faction conflicts
    
*   Living, breathing world
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#are-there-dynamic-villages)

Are there dynamic villages?

**Planned for Future Updates**

**Vision:**

*   Villages with relationships
    
*   NPC behaviors and routines
    
*   Village growth and development
    
*   Village defense and raids
    
*   Player interaction with communities
    

**Status:** Being designed and developed

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#how-do-chunks-and-entities-load)

How do chunks and entities load?

**Render Distance Based**

**Loading Rules:**

*   Entities load when in ANY player's render distance
    
*   Entities unload when ALL players are out of range
    
*   Chunks load/unload dynamically
    
*   Optimized for performance
    

**Benefits:**

*   Better server performance
    
*   Reduced memory usage
    
*   Smooth gameplay
    
*   Efficient resource management
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#can-i-share-world-generation-seeds)

Can I share world generation seeds?

**Yes - Shareable Seeds**

**Features:**

*   Enter custom seeds
    
*   Generate identical worlds
    
*   Share with friends
    
*   Community seed databases
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#development-philosophy)

Development Philosophy


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#release-strategy)

Release Strategy

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#what-is-the-priority-for-early-access)

What is the priority for Early Access?

**Adventure Mode First**

**Focus Areas:**

1.  Base game experience
    
2.  Core gameplay loops
    
3.  Adventure mode content
    
4.  Modding architecture (supports everything)
    

**Modding Support:**

*   Built alongside adventure mode
    
*   Same tools used internally
    
*   "Anything we do, you can do"
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#what-about-technical-debt)

What about technical debt?

**Acknowledged as Necessary**

**Approach:**

*   Some tech debt required for release
    
*   Commitment to continuous improvement
    
*   Transparent about limitations
    
*   Active post-launch refinement
    

**Philosophy:**

> _"Release first, improve continuously"_

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#how-often-will-hytale-be-updated)

How often will Hytale be updated?

**Very Frequent Updates**

**Cadence:**

*   Especially frequent post-launch
    
*   Bug fixes and improvements
    
*   New features and content
    
*   Community-driven priorities
    

**Commitment:**

*   Long-term support
    
*   Active development
    
*   Community feedback integration
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#what-is-the-versioning-policy)

What is the versioning policy?

**Always Latest Version**

**Server Flexibility:**

*   Official client always latest
    
*   Servers can run modified versions
    
*   Server source code available
    
*   Customize as needed
    

**Benefits:**

*   No fragmentation
    
*   Consistent client experience
    
*   Server flexibility
    
*   Modding freedom
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#community-focus)

**Yes - Planned for Community Contributors**

**Vision:**

*   Reward contributions
    
*   Strengthen ecosystem
    
*   Community-driven development
    
*   Recognize talent
    

**Timeline:** Takes time to set up properly

**Content:**

*   Official modding tutorials
    
*   Video guides
    
*   Written documentation
    
*   Partner collaborations
    

**Documentation:**

*   GitBook public documentation
    
*   Initially sparse
    
*   Expands based on community questions
    
*   Community contributions welcome

**Strong Commitment**

**Process:**

*   Active listening on Discord
    
*   Community-driven improvements
    
*   Feedback shapes development
    
*   Transparent communication
    

**Accountability:**

> _"Hold us accountable, demand answers, provide feedback"_ - Developers

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#what-are-the-system-requirements)

**Target:**

*   Lower-end hardware support
    
*   Reasonable requirements
    
*   Wide player base
    
*   Performance optimization
    

**Performance:**

*   Uncapped framerate
    
*   Multi-core support
    
*   Optimization focus

*   Used professionally by Hytale team

**Benefits:**

*   Contribute improvements
    
*   Deep customization

**Features:**

*   Full game experience offline
    
*   Local world saves
    
*   Multiplayer requires connection

**Optimization:**

*   Multi-core support
    
*   Performance focus
    
*   Accessible to lower-end hardware
    
*   Continuous optimization

Monetization & Legal


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#business-model)

Business Model

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#will-there-be-pay-to-win-mechanics)

Will there be pay-to-win mechanics?

**Absolutely Not - Firm Commitment**

**Policy:**

*   No pay-to-win mechanics
    
*   Cosmetics only
    
*   Low-price cosmetic packs
    
*   Support infrastructure costs
    

**Philosophy:**

> _"We are firmly against pay-to-win"_ - Hypixel Studios

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#what-cosmetics-will-be-available)

What cosmetics will be available?

**Low-Price Cosmetic Packs**

**Purpose:**

*   Support server infrastructure
    
*   Optional purchases
    
*   Customization options
    
*   No gameplay advantages
    

**Pricing:**

*   Affordable
    
*   No aggressive monetization
    
*   Player-first approach
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#what-about-server-monetization)

What about server monetization?

**EULA/TOS Being Finalized**

**Status:**

*   Server monetization policies being defined
    
*   Terms of Service in development
    
*   Balance between freedom and fairness
    
*   Details coming soon
    

**Hosting:**

*   No business agreements required
    
*   Day 1 server hosting available
    
*   Just comply with EULA/TOS
    

* * *

Current Limitations


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#technical-constraints)

Technical Constraints

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#can-i-use-custom-shaders)

Can I use custom shaders?

**Not Currently - Security Concern**

**Issue:**

*   No sandboxing solution yet
    
*   Security risk
    
*   Being researched
    

**Future:**

*   May be added if sandboxing solved
    
*   Community interest acknowledged
    
*   No timeline yet
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#are-ui-and-input-systems-limited)

Are UI and input systems limited?

**Currently Yes - Being Expanded**

**Status:**

*   Some limitations exist
    
*   Actively being improved
    
*   NoesisGUI transition in progress
    
*   More capabilities coming
    

**Timeline:** Continuous improvement

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#how-complete-is-the-documentation)

How complete is the documentation?

**Sparse Initially**

**Reality:**

*   Starting incomplete
    
*   Will improve over time
    
*   Community questions guide expansion
    
*   Contributions welcome
    

**Approach:**

*   Transparent about limitations
    
*   Honest about readiness
    
*   Commitment to improvement
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#can-clients-run-mods)

Can clients run mods?

**No - Security Design**

**Reason:**

*   No client-side code execution
    
*   Prevents exploits
    
*   Server controls everything
    
*   Security first
    

**Benefits:**

*   Safe for all players
    
*   No malware risk
    
*   Consistent experience
    
*   Server-controlled content
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/introduction/00-technical-insights#can-i-customize-player-nameplates)

Can I customize player nameplates?

**Currently Limited**

**Status:**

*   Limited customization options
    
*   Being improved
    
*   More options planned
    
*   Future updates

Long-Term Goals

**Core Commitments:**

1.  Security without compromising creativity
    
2.  Accessibility for all skill levels
    
3.  Continuous improvement
    
4.  Community-driven development
    
5.  Long-term support

# Setting Up a Local Server | Hytale Modding Documentation

Copy

    # Setting Up a Local Server
    
    **Source:** [Hytale Server Manual](https://support.hytale.com/hc/en-us/articles/45326769420827-Hytale-Server-Manual)  
    **Last Modified:** Friday, January 16, 2026 at 12:53 PM
    
    ---
    
    ## Overview
    
    This guide helps you set up a local Hytale server for testing mods, LAN play, or development on your machine.[file:12]
    
    ---
    
    ## Prerequisites
    
    Before you begin, ensure you have:
    - **Hytale** installed via the official launcher
    - **Java 25** from [Adoptium](https://adoptium.net/temurin/releases)
    - Basic command line/terminal knowledge[file:12]
    
    ---
    
    ## Step 1: Locating Hytale Server Files
    
    1. Open Hytale Launcher → **Settings** → **Open Directory**
    2. Go to: `%appdata%\Hytale\install\release\package\game\latest\`
    3. Copy **Server/** folder and **Assets.zip** to `C:\HytaleServer\`
    

C:\\HytaleServer ├── Server\\HytaleServer.jar └── Assets.zip

cd C:\\HytaleServer java -Xmx4G -jar Server\\HytaleServer.jar --assets Assets.zip

New-NetFirewallRule -DisplayName "Hytale Server" -Direction Inbound -Protocol UDP -LocalPort 5520 -Action Allow

**Key files:**

*   `config.json` - Server settings
    
*   `universe/worlds/*/config.json` - World settings
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/18-setting-up-local-server#installing-mods-on-your-server)

Installing Mods on Your Server

1.  Create `mods/` folder in server directory
    
2.  Drop `.zip` or `.jar` files into `mods/`
    
3.  Restart server
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/18-setting-up-local-server#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/18-setting-up-local-server#server-wont-start)

Server won't start

*   Verify: `java --version` shows OpenJDK 25
    
*   Use 4GB+ RAM: `-Xmx4G`
    
*   Check Assets.zip path
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/18-setting-up-local-server#cant-connect-to-server)

Can't connect to server

*   Use **UDP port 5520** (not 25565)
    
*   Allow UDP 5520 in firewall
    
*   Server must be authenticated
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/18-setting-up-local-server#port-already-in-use)

Port already in use

Kill process or change port with `--bind 0.0.0.0:25565`

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/18-setting-up-local-server#authentication-issues)

Authentication issues

*   Delete auth files
    
*   Retry `/auth login device`
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/18-setting-up-local-server#getting-help)

Getting Help

**Official Channels:**

*   **Server Manual:** [Hytale Server Manualarrow-up-right](https://support.hytale.com/hc/en-us/articles/45326769420827-Hytale-Server-Manual)
    
*   **Discord:** [Official Hytale Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/hytale)
    
*   **Blog:** [Hytale Newsarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news)
    

[PreviousHytale Modding Overviewchevron-left](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/getting-started/01-hytale-modding-overview)
[NextRunning a Dedicated Serverchevron-right](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/19-running-dedicated-server)

Last updated 1 day ago

*   [Installing Mods on Your Server](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/18-setting-up-local-server#installing-mods-on-your-server)
    
*   [Troubleshooting](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/18-setting-up-local-server#troubleshooting)
    
*   [Getting Help](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/18-setting-up-local-server#getting-help)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    
    ---
    
    ## Step 2: Launching the Server
    

Copy

    
    ---
    
    ## Step 3: Server Authentication
    
    ### You MUST authenticate your server!
    
    1. Run: `/auth login device`
    2. Visit printed URL + code in browser  
    3. Login with Hytale account
    4. Run: `/auth persistence Encrypted`
    
    **Never share your encrypted auth file!**[file:12]
    
    ---
    
    ## Step 4: Connecting to Your Server
    
    **Local:** `localhost:5520`  
    **LAN:** `192.168.x.x:5520`
    
    **In Hytale client:**
    1. **Play** → **Servers** → **Add Server**
    2. Enter address above
    3. Join!
    
    **Firewall (Windows):**

Copy

    
    ---
    
    ## Step 5: Basic Server Configuration
    
    Edit `config.json` (server stopped):
    ```json
    {
      "max-players": 10,
      "view-distance": 12
    }

Copy

    netstat -ano | findstr :5520

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Running a Dedicated Server | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [Running a Dedicated Serverarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/)
 **Last Modified:** Friday, January 16, 2026 at 08:00 AM

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/19-running-dedicated-server#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This guide covers setting up a dedicated Hytale server for 24/7 hosting, whether on a VPS, dedicated server, or home server machine.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/19-running-dedicated-server#prerequisites)

Prerequisites


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before you begin, ensure you have:

*   A server machine or VPS (recommended specifications below)
    
*   **Java 25** installed
    
*   Basic Linux/Windows server administration knowledge
    
*   Static IP or domain name (recommended)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/19-running-dedicated-server#recommended-server-specifications)

Recommended Server Specifications


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

\[Content to be added\]

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/19-running-dedicated-server#step-1-server-setup)

Step 1: Server Setup


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

\[Content to be added\]

* * *

\[Content to be added\]

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/19-running-dedicated-server#step-4-server-authentication)

Step 4: Server Authentication


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/19-running-dedicated-server#you-must-authenticate-your-server)

You MUST authenticate your server!

In order to allow players to connect to your dedicated server, you must authenticate it with Hytale. This is done by running the `auth login device` command in the server terminal.

Once authenticated, you can run the `auth persistence Encrypted` command to keep your server authenticated after restarting it.

**Never share your encrypted auth file!**

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/19-running-dedicated-server#step-5-configuring-server-settings)

# Server Tips & Optimization | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [Hytale Server Manualarrow-up-right](https://support.hytale.com/hc/en-us/articles/45326769420827-Hytale-Server-Manual)
 **Last Modified:** Friday, January 16, 2026 at 1:04 PM

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/23-tips-and-optimization#installing-mods)

Installing Mods


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Simple 3-step process:**

1.  Download `.zip` or `.jar` from [CurseForgearrow-up-right](https://www.curseforge.com/hytale)
    
2.  Drop into `mods/` folder
    
3.  Restart server
    

Copy

    📁 Server Folder
    └── mods/
        ├── MyMod.zip
        └── CoolPlugin.jar

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/23-tips-and-optimization#disable-sentry-crash-reporting)

Disable Sentry Crash Reporting


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> **Important:** Disable during plugin development

Copy

    java -jar HytaleServer.jar --assets Assets.zip --disable-sentry

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/23-tips-and-optimization#leverage-aot-cache)

Leverage AOT Cache


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Faster startup** with pre-trained cache:

[JEP-514arrow-up-right](https://openjdk.org/jeps/514)

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/23-tips-and-optimization#recommended-plugins)

Recommended Plugins


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Plugin

Purpose

[Nitrado:WebServerarrow-up-right](https://github.com/nitrado/hytale-plugin-webserver)

Web APIs

[Nitrado:Queryarrow-up-right](https://github.com/nitrado/hytale-plugin-query)

Server status

[PerformanceSaverarrow-up-right](https://github.com/nitrado/hytale-plugin-performance-saver)

Dynamic view distance

[PrometheusExporterarrow-up-right](https://github.com/apexhosting/hytale-plugin-prometheus)

Performance metrics

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/23-tips-and-optimization#view-distance-tuning)

View Distance Tuning


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**RAM Usage Guide:**

**vs Minecraft:**

Chunks

Blocks

**384**
