[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/23-tips-and-optimization#multiserver-architecture)

Multiserver Architecture


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**No BungeeCord needed** - native routing.

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/23-tips-and-optimization#player-referral)

Player Referral

**⚠️ Sign payloads** (HMAC required)

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/23-tips-and-optimization#connection-redirect)

Connection Redirect

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/23-tips-and-optimization#quick-commands)

Quick Commands


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use Case

Command

Development

`java -jar HytaleServer.jar --assets Assets.zip --disable-sentry`

Production

`java -Xmx6G -XX:AOTCache=HytaleServer.aot -jar HytaleServer.jar --assets Assets.zip`

Custom Port

`java -jar HytaleServer.jar --bind 0.0.0.0:25565 --assets Assets.zip`

Copy

    java -XX:AOTCache=HytaleServer.aot -jar HytaleServer.jar --assets Assets.zip

Copy

    8 chunks   → 2-4GB RAM  (4 players)
    12 chunks  → 4-6GB RAM  (8-12 players) ✅ RECOMMENDED
    16 chunks  → 8GB+ RAM   (Risky!)

Copy

    PlayerRef.referToServer("lobby.com", 5520, data);

Copy

    PlayerSetupConnectEvent.referToServer("eu.server", 5520);

# Server Commands & Permissions | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [Server Commands & Permissionsarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/)
 **Last Modified:** Friday, January 16, 2026 at 08:00 AM

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/22-server-commands-permissions#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This guide covers all available server commands, permission systems, and how to manage operator status and player permissions on your Hytale server.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/22-server-commands-permissions#basic-server-commands)

Basic Server Commands


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

\[Content to be added\]

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/22-server-commands-permissions#authentication-commands)

Authentication Commands


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/22-server-commands-permissions#auth-login-device)

auth login device

Authenticates your server with Hytale. This command prints a URL that you can use to authenticate the server using your Hytale account.

Copy

    auth login device

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/22-server-commands-permissions#auth-persistence-encrypted)

auth persistence Encrypted

Keeps your server authenticated after restarting. Run this after authenticating once.

**Warning:** Never share your encrypted auth file!

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/22-server-commands-permissions#player-management-commands)

# Future Server Additions | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [Hytale Server Manualarrow-up-right](https://support.hytale.com/hc/en-us/articles/45326769420827-Hytale-Server-Manual)
 **Last Modified:** Friday, January 16, 2026 at 12:56 PM

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/24-future-additions#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Upcoming Hytale server features will enhance discoverability, social gameplay, monetization, and operations for server administrators.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/24-future-additions#server-and-minigame-discovery)

Server & Minigame Discovery


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Status:** Planned for main menu integration.

**Features:**

*   In-game server browser for servers and minigames
    
*   Server operators opt-in to promote content
    
*   Real-time player discovery catalogue
    

**Listing Requirements:**

Requirement

Description

Server Operator Guidelines

Must follow Hytale community standards

Self-Rating

Accurate content ratings for parental controls

Enforcement

Violations lead to delisting

**Player Count Verification:**

*   Uses client telemetry (not server-reported)
    
*   Prevents count spoofing
    
*   Unverified counts shown for manually added servers
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/24-future-additions#parties-system)

Parties System


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Status:** In development.

**Features:**

*   Cross-server party persistence
    
*   Party-aware server browsing
    
*   Visible party size limits before joining
    

**Integration:**

*   Groups browse/join servers together
    
*   Seamless social experience across Hytale ecosystem
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/24-future-additions#integrated-payment-system)

Integrated Payment System


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Status:** Planned client integration.

**Server Operator Benefits:**

*   Accept payments without external services
    
*   No payment infrastructure required
    
*   Secure transactions via Hytale
    

**Player Benefits:**

*   In-game payments (no external websites)
    
*   Fully secure and traceable
    
*   Ecosystem-contained transactions
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/24-future-additions#srv-record-support)

SRV Record Support


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Status:** Unsupported, under evaluation.

**What it enables:**

*   Connect via `play.example.com` (no port needed)
    
*   DNS resolves address + port automatically
    

**Current Limitations:**

*   No production-ready C# SRV library
    
*   Full DNS client adds complexity/risk
    
*   Revisit when suitable solution available
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/24-future-additions#first-party-api-endpoints)

First-Party API Endpoints


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Status:** Planned for authenticated servers.

**Core Endpoints:**

Endpoint

Description

UUID ↔ Name Lookup

Single/bulk player name resolution

Game Version

Protocol/version checking

Player Profile

Cosmetics, avatar, public data

Server Telemetry

Status reporting for discovery

Report

ToS violation reporting

Payments

Built-in payment processing

**Under Consideration:**

Endpoint

Description

Global Sanctions

Platform-level ban checks

Friends List

Social features (permissioned)

Webhook Subscriptions

Event notifications

**Design Goals:**

*   Generous rate limits + bulk endpoints
    
*   Server authentication required
    
*   Versioned APIs with deprecation windows
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/server-administration/24-future-additions#getting-help)

Getting Help


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Official Channels:**

*   **Server Manual:** [Hytale Server Manualarrow-up-right](https://support.hytale.com/hc/en-us/articles/45326769420827-Hytale-Server-Manual)
    
*   **Discord:** [Official Hytale Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/hytale)
    
*   **Blog:** [Hytale Newsarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news)

# Getting Started with Packs | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [Getting Started with Packsarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/)

**Last Modified:** Friday, January 16, 2026 at 12:47 PM

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/02-getting-started-with-packs#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This guide walks you through creating your first Hytale Pack. Packs are asset/content packs that allow you to add new blocks, items, mobs, and behavior to Hytale without requiring coding knowledge.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/02-getting-started-with-packs#step-1-creating-a-folder)

Step 1: Creating a Folder


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

First, create a folder for your Pack:

**Path:** `./AppData/Roaming/Hytale/UserData/Mods/YourPackName`

Replace `YourPackName` with the desired name of your Pack.

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/02-getting-started-with-packs#example)

Example:

Copy

    C:\Users\YourUsername\AppData\Roaming\Hytale\UserData\Mods\MyFirstPack
    

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/02-getting-started-with-packs#asset-editor-alternative)

Asset Editor (Alternative)


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use the in-game Asset Editor for a quicker start:

1.  Launch Hytale and create a new **Creative World**.
    
2.  Grant yourself OP status by typing `/op self` in chat.
    
3.  Open your **Inventory**, then navigate to **Creative Tools** > **Assets** > **Asset Editor**.
    
4.  In the Asset Editor, click the three dots in the top left and select **Add Pack**.
    
5.  Enter your pack details.
    
6.  Proceed to Step 3.
    

> **Note:** Check our [YouTube Tutorialsarrow-up-right](https://www.google.com/search?q=00-youtube-tutorials.md)
>  for more on the Asset Editor.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/02-getting-started-with-packs#step-2-manifest-file)

Step 2: Manifest File


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create a `manifest.json` file in your Pack folder. This file contains metadata about your Pack.

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/02-getting-started-with-packs#manifest-template)

Manifest Template:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/02-getting-started-with-packs#manifest-fields-explained)

Manifest Fields Explained:

Field

Description

Required

`Group`

Your organization or group name

Yes

`Name`

The name of your Pack

Yes

`Version`

Version number (semantic versioning)

Yes

`Description`

A brief description of what your Pack does

Yes

`Authors`

Array of author information

Yes

`Website`

Your website or project page

Optional

`ServerVersion`

Compatible server version (`*` for all)

Yes

`Dependencies`

Packs required for this to work

Optional

`OptionalDependencies`

Packs that enhance but aren't required

Optional

`DisabledByDefault`

Whether Pack loads automatically

Optional

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/02-getting-started-with-packs#step-3-common-and-server-folders)

Step 3: Common and Server Folders


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create two main folders inside your Pack directory:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/02-getting-started-with-packs#folder-structure)

Folder Structure:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/02-getting-started-with-packs#common-folder)

Common Folder

**Path:** `./AppData/Roaming/Hytale/UserData/Packs/YourPackName/Common`

**Handles:**

*   Models
    
*   Textures
    
*   Visual assets
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/02-getting-started-with-packs#server-folder)

Server Folder

**Path:** `./AppData/Roaming/Hytale/UserData/Packs/YourPackName/Server`

**Handles:**

*   Item creation
    
*   Block creation
    
*   Translations
    
*   Particle creation
    
*   Game logic and behavior
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/02-getting-started-with-packs#complete-folder-structure-example)

Complete Folder Structure Example


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> **Note:** This shows key folders; full structures vary. For a complete overview:
> 
> 1.  Open the Hytale launcher.
>     
> 2.  Click **Settings** (top left).
>     
> 3.  Select **Open Directory**.
>     
> 4.  Navigate to `install\release\package\game\latest` and explore `Assets.zip`.
>     

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/02-getting-started-with-packs#activating-your-pack)

Activating Your Pack


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use your Pack in Hytale:

1.  Open Hytale.
    
2.  Go to the **Worlds** tab.
    
3.  Right-click the target world.
    
4.  Toggle on your Pack.
    
5.  Enter the world to test changes.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/02-getting-started-with-packs#getting-help)

Getting Help


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Official Channels:**

*   **Discord:** [Official Hytale Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/hytale)
    
*   **Blog:** [Hytale Newsarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news)
    

Would you like me to clean up any other guides in this series for you?

Copy

    {
      "Group": "YourGroupName",
      "Name": "PackName",
      "Version": "1.0.0",
      "Description": "Add the pack description here",
      "Authors": [\
        {\
          "Name": "AuthorName",\
          "Email": "example@example.com",\
          "Url": "https://your-url.com"\
        }\
      ],
      "Website": "https://your-website.com",
      "ServerVersion": "*",
      "Dependencies": {},
      "OptionalDependencies": {},
      "DisabledByDefault": false
    }
    

Copy

    ./AppData/Roaming/Hytale/UserData/Packs/YourPackName/
    |-- manifest.json
    |-- Common/
    `-- Server/
    

Copy

    MyFirstPack/
    |-- manifest.json
    |-- Common/
    |   |-- BlockTextures/
    |   |-- Icons/
    |   `-- Models/
    `-- Server/
        |-- Item/
        |   |-- Items/
        |   `-- Category/
        |-- Languages/
        |   `-- en-US/
        `-- Block/

# Block State Changing | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [Block State Changingarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/)

**Last Modified:** Friday, January 9, 2026 at 12:01 PM

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is a basic beginner's guide on how to modify block state changes and cycling. Block states allow you to create blocks that can change appearance, behavior, or properties when interacted with, similar to doors, lights, or buttons in the game.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#what-are-block-states)

What are Block States?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Block states allow a single block to have multiple configurations or modes:

*   **Lamps** that can be on or off
    
*   **Doors** that can be open or closed
    
*   **Machines** that can be active or inactive
    
*   **Any block** with multiple visual or functional states
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#step-1-select-your-block)

Step 1: Select Your Block


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

First, locate your block definition file:

**Path:** `Packs/YourPackName/Server/Item/Items/your_block.json`

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#step-2-create-an-interaction)

Step 2: Create an Interaction


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Define an interaction that will trigger the state change. This tells the game what should happen when the player interacts with the block.

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#interaction-structure)

Interaction Structure:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#interaction-properties-explained)

Interaction Properties Explained:

Property

Description

`"Use"`

The interaction type (player right-clicks/uses the block)

`"Type": "ChangeState"`

Tells the game to change the block's state

`"Changes"`

Maps current state -> next state

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#state-cycling-logic)

State Cycling Logic:

This creates a toggle behavior: On -> Off -> On -> Off...

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#step-3-define-states)

Step 3: Define States


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Now define what each state looks like and behaves like:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#state-definition-structure)

State Definition Structure:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#state-properties)

State Properties:

Property

Description

Example

`InteractionHint`

Tooltip shown when hovering

`"interactionHints.turnoff"`

`CustomModel`

Model file for this state

`"Blocks/model_one.blockymodel"`

`CustomModelTexture`

Texture(s) for this state

Array of texture objects

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#complete-example-block)

Complete Example Block


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here's a full example of a block with state changing:

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#advanced-state-features)

Advanced State Features


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can add additional properties to each state:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#sounds)

Sounds

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#animations)

Animations

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#particles)

Particles

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#multiple-states-beyond-on-off)

Multiple States (Beyond On/Off)


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can have more than two states:

Then define all three states:

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#interaction-hints-translation)

Interaction Hints Translation


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Remember to add translations for your interaction hints:

**Path:** `YourPackName/Server/Languages/en-US/interactionHints.lang`

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#required-files)

Required Files


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For a state-changing block with custom models, you need:

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#testing-your-state-changing-block)

Testing Your State-Changing Block


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Enable your Pack in a world
    
2.  Place the block
    
3.  Observe its initial state (default)
    
4.  Right-click/use the block
    
5.  Verify it changes to the next state
    
6.  Check that the model/texture updates
    
7.  Verify the interaction hint displays correctly
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#states-dont-change)

States don't change:

*   Verify `"Type": "ChangeState"` is set correctly
    
*   Check that state names match in `Changes` and `Definitions`
    
*   Ensure interaction type is correct (`"Use"`)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#wrong-initial-state)

Wrong initial state:

*   Check `"default"` value in `Changes`
    
*   Verify the default state is defined in `Definitions`
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#models-textures-dont-update)

Models/textures don't update:

*   Verify model paths are correct for each state
    
*   Check that texture paths exist
    
*   Ensure models are properly formatted `.blockymodel` files
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#interaction-hints-dont-show)

Interaction hints don't show:

*   Verify translation keys exist in `interactionHints.lang`
    
*   Check that language file is in correct location
    
*   Ensure no typos in translation keys
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/04-block-state-changing#getting-help)

Getting Help


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Discord:** [Official Hytale Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/hytale)
    
*   **Blog:** [Hytale Newsarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news)

Copy

    "Interactions": {
      "Use": {
        "Interactions": [\
          {\
            "Type": "ChangeState",\
            "Changes": {\
              "default": "Off",\
              "On": "Off",\
              "Off": "On"\
            }\
          }\
        ]
      }
    }
    

Copy

    "Changes": {
      "default": "Off",  // Initial state when placed
      "On": "Off",       // When "On", change to "Off"
      "Off": "On"        // When "Off", change to "On"
    }
    

Copy

    "State": {
      "Definitions": {
        "On": {
          "InteractionHint": "interactionHints.turnoff",
          "CustomModel": "Blocks/model_one.blockymodel",
          "CustomModelTexture": [\
            {\
              "Texture": "Blocks/Texture/textureone.png"\
            }\
          ]
        },
        "Off": {
          "InteractionHint": "interactionHints.turnon",
          "CustomModel": "Blocks/model_two.blockymodel",
          "CustomModelTexture": [\
            {\
              "Texture": "Blocks/Texture/textureone.png"\
            }\
          ]
        }
      }
    }
    

Copy

    {
      "TranslationProperties": {
        "Name": "server.Toggle_Block.name"
      },
      "MaxStack": 100,
      "Icon": "Icons/ItemsGenerated/Toggle_Block.png",
      "Categories": [\
        "Blocks.Decoration"\
      ],
      "BlockType": {
        "DrawType": "Model",
        "CustomModel": "Blocks/model_one.blockymodel",
        "CustomModelTexture": [\
          {\
            "Texture": "Blocks/your_texture.png"\
          }\
        ],
        
        "Interactions": {
          "Use": {
            "Interactions": [\
              {\
                "Type": "ChangeState",\
                "Changes": {\
                  "default": "Off",\
                  "On": "Off",\
                  "Off": "On"\
                }\
              }\
            ]
          }
        },
        
        "State": {
          "Definitions": {
            "On": {
              "InteractionHint": "interactionHints.turnoff",
              "CustomModel": "Blocks/model_one.blockymodel",
              "CustomModelTexture": [\
                {\
                  "Texture": "Blocks/Texture/textureone.png"\
                }\
              ]
            },
            "Off": {
              "InteractionHint": "interactionHints.turnon",
              "CustomModel": "Blocks/model_two.blockymodel",
              "CustomModelTexture": [\
                {\
                  "Texture": "Blocks/Texture/textureone.png"\
                }\
              ]
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }

      "InteractionHint": "interactionHints.turnoff",
      "CustomModel": "Blocks/model_one.blockymodel",
      "BlockSoundSetId": "Metal_On"
    }

      "InteractionHint": "interactionHints.turnoff",
      "CustomModel": "Blocks/model_one.blockymodel",
      "CustomModelAnimation": "Blocks/Animations/Light_On.blockyanim"
    }

      "ParticleColor": "#ffff00"
    }

      "Use": {
        "Interactions": [\

              "default": "State1",\

    turnoff = Turn Off

    |-- Common/
    |   `-- Blocks/
    |       |-- model_one.blockymodel
    |       |-- model_two.blockymodel
    |       `-- Texture/
    |           `-- textureone.png
    `-- Server/
        |-- Item/
        |   `-- Items/
        |       `-- your_block.json
        `-- Languages/
            `-- en-US/
                `-- interactionHints.lang

# Item Categories | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [Item Categoriesarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/)

**Last Modified:** Friday, January 9, 2026 at 12:01 PM

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Item Categories are the different tabs shown in the Creative Menu. This guide provides a basic introduction to creating your own categories and subcategories for organizing your custom items and blocks.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#what-are-item-categories)

What are Item Categories?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Item Categories allow you to:

*   Create custom tabs in the Creative Menu
    
*   Organize items and blocks logically
    
*   Add subcategories for better organization
    
*   Customize icons for each category
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#step-1-creating-the-category-file)

Step 1: Creating the Category File


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create a JSON file for your custom category:

**Path:** `AppData/Roaming/Hytale/UserData/Packs/YourPackName/Server/Item/Category/CreativeLibrary/MyItemCategory.json`

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#category-template)

Category Template:

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#category-properties-explained)

Category Properties Explained


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#main-category-properties)

Main Category Properties

Property

Description

Example

`Id`

Unique identifier for the category

`"MyCategory"`

`Name`

Translation key for tooltip text

`"ui.itemcategory.mycategory"`

`Icon`

Path to the category icon

`"Icons/ItemCategories/MyCategory.png"`

`Order`

Position in Creative Menu (lower = left)

`6`

`Children`

Array of subcategories

See template above

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#subcategory-properties-children)

Subcategory Properties (Children)

Each child/subcategory has:

*   `Id` - Unique identifier for the subcategory
    
*   `Name` - Translation key for the subcategory tooltip
    
*   `Icon` - Path to the subcategory icon
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#step-2-adding-translations)

Step 2: Adding Translations


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Define the display names for your categories by creating translation files:

**Path:** `YourPackName/Server/Languages/en-US/ui.lang`

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#translation-format)

Translation Format:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#key-points)

Key Points:

*   Translation keys in JSON start with `"ui."` but the `.lang` file omits this prefix
    
*   The text after `=` is what displays when hovering over the category icon
    
*   Create files for other languages (e.g., `es-ES/ui.lang`) for internationalization
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#step-3-adding-icons)

Step 3: Adding Icons


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create icon images for your categories:

**Main Category Icon Path:** `YourPackName/Common/Icons/ItemCategories/MyCategory.png`

**Subcategory Icon Paths:** `YourPackName/Common/Icons/ItemCategories/My_Example_Category.png`

`YourPackName/Common/Icons/ItemCategories/My_Example_Category_Two.png`

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#icon-requirements)

Icon Requirements:

*   **Format:** PNG with transparency support
    
*   **Recommended Size:** 32x32 pixels
    
*   **Style:** Should match Hytale's UI aesthetic
    
*   **Naming:** Must match exactly the path in your JSON file
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#step-4-adding-blocks-items-to-categories)

Step 4: Adding Blocks/Items to Categories


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To add your custom blocks or items to your new categories, edit the item/block JSON file:

**Path:** `YourPackName/Server/Item/Items/your_block.json`

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#add-category-reference)

Add Category Reference:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#category-path-format)

Category Path Format:

*   **Main Category Only:** `"MyCategory"`
    
*   **Subcategory:** `"MyCategory.Example_Category"`
    
*   **Multiple Categories:** Add multiple strings to the array
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#example-multiple-categories)

Example - Multiple Categories:

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#finding-vanilla-category-names)

Finding Vanilla Category Names


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use Vanilla categories in your items, look in the game's asset files:

**Path:** `Assets/Server/Item/Category/CreativeLibrary`

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#common-vanilla-categories)

Common Vanilla Categories:

*   `Blocks.Rocks`
    
*   `Blocks.Wood`
    
*   `Blocks.Nature`
    
*   `Items.Tools`
    
*   `Items.Weapons`
    
*   `Items.Food`
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#complete-folder-structure-example)

Complete Folder Structure Example


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#advanced-category-order)

Advanced: Category Order


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `Order` property determines the position of your category in the Creative Menu:

*   **Lower numbers** = Further left
    
*   **Higher numbers** = Further right
    
*   **Vanilla categories** typically use orders 0-5
    
*   **Custom categories** should use 6+
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#example-order)

Example Order:

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#testing-your-categories)

Testing Your Categories


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Enable your Pack in a world
    
2.  Enter the world
    
3.  Open your inventory in Creative Mode
    
4.  Look for your custom category icon(s) in the Creative Menu
    
5.  Click the icon to see your subcategories
    
6.  Verify items appear in the correct subcategories
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#category-doesnt-appear)

Category doesn't appear:

*   Verify JSON syntax is valid
    
*   Check that icon paths are correct
    
*   Ensure translation file exists
    
*   Verify Pack is enabled in world
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#icon-is-missing)

Icon is missing:

*   Check icon file exists at specified path
    
*   Verify PNG format
    
*   Ensure path in JSON matches file location exactly
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#items-dont-appear-in-category)

Items don't appear in category:

*   Verify category ID matches in both files
    
*   Check subcategory path format: `"MainCategory.SubCategory"`
    
*   Ensure item JSON includes `Categories` array
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#tooltip-shows-translation-key)

Tooltip shows translation key:

*   Check `ui.lang` file exists
    
*   Verify translation key matches (without `ui.` prefix)
    
*   Ensure no typos in the key
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/05-item-categories#getting-help)

Getting Help


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Official Channels:**

*   **Discord:** [Official Hytale Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/hytale)
    
*   **Blog:** [Hytale Newsarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news)

        {\
          "Id": "Example_Category_Two",\
          "Name": "ui.itemcategory.example_category_two",\
          "Icon": "Icons/ItemCategories/My_Example_Category_Two.png"\
        }\
      ]
    }

    itemcategory.mycategory = My Custom Category
    itemcategory.example_category = Example Tab One
    itemcategory.example_category_two = Example Tab Two

    {
      "TranslationProperties": {
        "Name": "server.Your_Block.name"
      },

        "MyCategory.Example_Category"\
      ],
      // ... rest of block properties
    }

      "MyCategory.Example_Category",\
      "Blocks.Rocks",\
      "MyCategory.Example_Category_Two"\
    ]

# Adding a Block | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [Adding a Blockarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/)

**Last Modified:** Friday, January 9, 2026 at 12:01 PM

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This guide teaches you how to add a custom block to Hytale using Packs. You'll learn how to create the block definition, add textures, and modify properties using the Asset Editor.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#prerequisites)

Prerequisites


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before starting, ensure you have:

*   Created a Pack folder structure (see "Getting Started with Packs")
    
*   A `manifest.json` file in your Pack root
    
*   `Common/` and `Server/` folders created
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#step-1-creating-the-block-manifest-file)

Step 1: Creating the Block Manifest File


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create a JSON file for your block in the Items directory:

**Path:** `./AppData/Roaming/Hytale/UserData/Packs/YourPackName/Server/Item/Items/your_block.json`

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#block-manifest-template)

Block Manifest Template:

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#block-properties-explained)

Block Properties Explained


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#top-level-properties)

Top-Level Properties

Property

Description

Example

`TranslationProperties.Name`

Translation key for block name

`"server.Example_Block.name"`

`MaxStack`

Maximum stack size in inventory

`100`

`Icon`

Path to inventory icon

`"Icons/ItemsGenerated/Example_Block.png"`

`Categories`

Creative menu categories

`["Blocks.Rocks"]`

`PlayerAnimationsId`

Animation set when placing

`"Block"`

`Set`

Block set identifier

`"Rock_Stone"`

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#blocktype-properties)

BlockType Properties

Property

Description

Options/Example

`Material`

Block material type

`"Solid"`, `"Liquid"`, `"Gas"`

`DrawType`

Rendering method

`"Cube"`, `"Cross"`, `"Model"`

`Group`

Block group for behavior

`"Stone"`, `"Wood"`, `"Dirt"`

`Flags`

Special block flags

`{}` (varies by block type)

`ParticleColor`

Color of break particles

`"#aeae8c"` (hex color)

`BlockSoundSetId`

Sound set for interactions

`"Stone"`, `"Wood"`, `"Grass"`

`BlockBreakingDecalId`

Breaking animation overlay

`"Breaking_Decals_Rock"`

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#gathering-properties)

Gathering Properties

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#texture-properties)

Texture Properties

**Alternative - Different Textures Per Side:**

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#step-2-creating-texture-files)

Step 2: Creating Texture Files


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create texture files in the Common folder:

**Texture Path:** `./AppData/Roaming/Hytale/UserData/Packs/YourPackName/Common/BlockTextures/your_block_texture.png`

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#texture-requirements)

Texture Requirements:

*   **Format:** PNG
    
*   **Recommended Size:** 16x16 or 32x32 pixels
    
*   **Transparency:** Supported (for non-solid blocks)
    
*   **Naming:** Match the path in your block JSON
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#icon-path)

Icon Path:

Also create an icon for the inventory:

**Icon Path:** `./AppData/Roaming/Hytale/UserData/Packs/YourPackName/Common/Icons/ItemsGenerated/Example_Block.png`

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#step-3-creating-translation-file)

Step 3: Creating Translation File


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create a translation file to define the block's display name:

**Path:** `./AppData/Roaming/Hytale/UserData/Packs/YourPackName/Server/Languages/en-US/server.lang`

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#translation-format)

Translation Format:

The key (`Example_Block.name`) must match the `TranslationProperties.Name` in your block JSON (without the `"server."` prefix).

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#multiple-languages)

Multiple Languages:

Create additional `.lang` files for other languages:

*   `es-ES/server.lang` - Spanish
    
*   `fr-FR/server.lang` - French
    
*   `de-DE/server.lang` - German
    
*   etc.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#step-4-modify-in-asset-editor)

Step 4: Modify in Asset Editor


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Now you can visually edit your block using the in-game Asset Editor:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#steps-to-access-asset-editor)

Steps to Access Asset Editor:

1.  **Add Pack to World:**
    

*   Open Hytale
    
*   Visit the "Worlds" tab
    
*   Right-click on your world
    
*   Toggle on your Pack
    

1.  **Enter the World:**
    

*   Join the world with your Pack enabled
    

1.  **Open Asset Editor:**
    

*   Open your inventory
    
*   Click on the "Creation Tools" tab
    
*   Click on "Asset Editor"
    

1.  **Edit Your Block:**
    

*   Select your Pack from the list
    
*   Find your block in the items list
    
*   Modify any settings you desire
    
*   Changes are saved automatically
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#what-you-can-edit-in-asset-editor)

What You Can Edit in Asset Editor:

*   Material properties
    
*   Breaking behavior
    
*   Sounds
    
*   Particle effects
    
*   Textures (paths)
    
*   Drop items
    
*   Stack size
    
*   Categories
    
*   And much more!
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#complete-folder-structure-example)

Complete Folder Structure Example


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#testing-your-block)

Testing Your Block


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Launch Hytale with your Pack enabled
    
2.  Open Creative Mode
    
3.  Open your inventory
    
4.  Find your block in the category you specified
    
5.  Place it in the world
    
6.  Test breaking it to verify drops and sounds
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#block-doesnt-appear-in-game)

Block doesn't appear in game:

*   Verify `manifest.json` is correct
    
*   Check that Pack is enabled in world settings
    
*   Ensure JSON syntax is valid (use a JSON validator)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#texture-is-missing-pink)

Texture is missing/pink:

*   Verify texture path matches JSON exactly
    
*   Check texture file exists at specified path
    
*   Ensure texture is PNG format
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#translation-shows-key-instead-of-name)

Translation shows key instead of name:

*   Verify translation key matches in JSON and `.lang` file
    
*   Check that `en-US` folder and `server.lang` file exist
    
*   Ensure no typos in translation key
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/03-adding-a-block#getting-help)

Getting Help


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Discord:** [Official Hytale Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/hytale)
    
*   **Blog:** [Hytale Newsarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news)

    {
      "TranslationProperties": {
        "Name": "server.Example_Block.name"
      },
      "MaxStack": 100,
      "Icon": "Icons/ItemsGenerated/Example_Block.png",
      "Categories": [\
        "Blocks.Rocks"\
      ],
      "PlayerAnimationsId": "Block",
      "Set": "Rock_Stone",
      "BlockType": {
        "Material": "Solid",
        "DrawType": "Cube",
        "Group": "Stone",
        "Flags": {},
        "Gathering": {
          "Breaking": {
            "GatherType": "Rocks",
            "ItemId": "Rock_Stone_Cobble"
          }
        },
        "BlockParticleSetId": "Stone",
        "Textures": [\
          {\
            "All": "BlockTextures/Example_Block.png"\
          }\
        ],
        "ParticleColor": "#aeae8c",
        "BlockSoundSetId": "Stone",
        "BlockBreakingDecalId": "Breaking_Decals_Rock"
      },
      "ResourceTypes": [\
        {\
          "Id": "Rock"\
        }\
      ]
    }
    

Copy

    "Gathering": {
      "Breaking": {
        "GatherType": "Rocks",    // Tool type required
        "ItemId": "Rock_Stone_Cobble"  // Item dropped when broken
      }
    }
    

Copy

    "Textures": [\
      {\
        "All": "BlockTextures/Example_Block.png"  // Same texture all sides\
      }\
    ]
    

Copy

    "Textures": [\
      {\
        "Top": "BlockTextures/Example_Block_Top.png",\
        "Bottom": "BlockTextures/Example_Block_Bottom.png",\
        "Sides": "BlockTextures/Example_Block_Sides.png"\
      }\
    ]
    

Copy

    Example_Block.name = Example Block
    

Copy

    YourPackName/
    |-- manifest.json
    |-- Common/
    |   |-- BlockTextures/
    |   |   `-- Example_Block.png
    |   `-- Icons/
    |       `-- ItemsGenerated/
    |           `-- Example_Block.png
    `-- Server/
        |-- Item/
        |   `-- Items/
        |       `-- your_block.json
        `-- Languages/
            `-- en-US/
                `-- server.lang

# Block Animations | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [Block Animationsarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/)

**Last Modified:** Friday, January 9, 2026 at 12:01 PM

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#overview)

Overview


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This guide explains how to add animations to blocks in Hytale. Animations can make your blocks come alive with moving parts, opening mechanisms, or any other dynamic movement.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#prerequisites)

Prerequisites


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Basic understanding of block states (see "Block State Changing" guide)
    
*   Blockbench installed ([https://www.blockbench.net/arrow-up-right](https://www.blockbench.net/)
    )
    
*   A block model with named groups
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#what-can-be-animated)

What Can Be Animated?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Block animations can modify:

*   **Position** - Move elements in X, Y, Z coordinates
    
*   **Orientation** - Rotate elements
    
*   **ShapeStretch** - Stretch or scale elements
    
*   **ShapeVisible** - Show or hide elements
    
*   **ShapeUvOffset** - Animate textures (advanced)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#step-1-add-animation-to-block-state)

Step 1: Add Animation to Block State


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

First, reference your animation file in the block's state definition:

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#step-2-create-groups-in-blockbench)

Step 2: Create Groups in Blockbench


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Open your block model in Blockbench:

1.  **Create a Group:**
    

*   In Blockbench, create a new group
    
*   Give it a descriptive name (e.g., "Water", "Door", "Drawer")
    
*   This group name will be referenced in your animation file
    

1.  **Add Elements:**
    

*   Place the elements you want to animate inside the group
    
*   You can have multiple elements in one group
    
*   All elements in the group will animate together
    

1.  **Export:**
    

*   Export as `.blockymodel` format for Hytale
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#step-3-create-animation-file)

Step 3: Create Animation File


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create a `.blockyanim` file in your Pack's animation folder:

**Path:** `YourPackName/Common/Blocks/Animations/Rising_Water.blockyanim`

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#basic-animation-structure)

Basic Animation Structure:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#animation-properties)

Animation Properties:

Property

Description

Example

`formatVersion`

Animation format version

`1`

`duration`

Animation length in ticks

`50` (2.5 seconds)

`holdLastKeyframe`

Whether to hold at final position

`true` or `false`

`nodeAnimations`

Object containing group animations

See below

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#animation-types)

Animation Types


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#position-animation)

Position Animation

Moves elements in 3D space:

**This example:** Moves the element 8.5 units up on the Y-axis over 50 ticks.

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#orientation-animation-rotation)

Orientation Animation (Rotation)

Rotates elements using quaternions:

**Note:** Quaternions are complex. Common rotation values:

*   **No rotation:** `{x:0, y:0, z:0, w:1}`
    
*   **90° Y-axis:** `{x:0, y:0.707, z:0, w:0.707}`
    
*   **180° Y-axis:** `{x:0, y:1, z:0, w:0}`
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#example-1-rising-water-animation)

Example 1: Rising Water Animation


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This animation makes water rise from 0 to 8.5 units upward:

**File:** `Rising_Water.blockyanim`

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#example-2-wardrobe-opening-animation)

Example 2: Wardrobe Opening Animation


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A complex example with multiple animated groups (doors, knockers, drawer):

**File:** `Wardrobe_Open.blockyanim`

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#breakdown-of-wardrobe-animation)

Breakdown of Wardrobe Animation:

*   **Door-L:** Left door swings open (rotates on Y-axis)
    
*   **Door-R:** Right door swings open (opposite direction)
    
*   **Drawer:** Pulls out (moves on Z-axis)
    
*   **Door-Knocker:** Bounces back and forth (multiple rotation keyframes)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#keyframe-properties)

Keyframe Properties


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each keyframe contains:

Property

Description

`time`

When this keyframe occurs (in ticks)

`delta`

The transformation values

`interpolationType`

How to transition (`"smooth"`, `"linear"`, `"step"`)

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#interpolation-types)

Interpolation Types:

*   **smooth:** Gradual acceleration/deceleration (natural)
    
*   **linear:** Constant speed (mechanical)
    
*   **step:** Instant change (no interpolation)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#complete-file-structure)

Complete File Structure


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#tips-for-creating-animations)

Tips for Creating Animations


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Start Simple:** Begin with single-axis position animations
    
2.  **Use Vanilla as Reference:** Look at wardrobe, door, and chest animations
    
3.  **Plan Timing:** Map out when each group should start/stop moving
    
4.  **Test Iteratively:** Test in-game frequently, adjust values
    
5.  **Empty Arrays:** Use `[]` for animation types you don't need
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#testing-your-animations)

Testing Your Animations


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Enable your Pack in a world
    
2.  Place the animated block
    
3.  Trigger the state change (e.g., right-click)
    
4.  Observe the animation
    
5.  Adjust timing and delta values as needed
    
6.  Reload the Pack to see changes
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#animation-doesnt-play)

Animation doesn't play:

*   Verify animation file path in block JSON
    
*   Check that group names match exactly (case-sensitive)
    
*   Ensure `.blockyanim` extension is correct
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#animation-is-choppy)

Animation is choppy:

*   Increase duration for smoother movement
    
*   Use "smooth" interpolation instead of "linear"
    
*   Add more intermediate keyframes
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#wrong-elements-animate)

Wrong elements animate:

*   Check group names in Blockbench
    
*   Verify correct elements are in the group
    
*   Ensure animation references the right group name
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#animation-plays-backwards)

Animation plays backwards:

*   Check time values increase correctly
    
*   Verify keyframes are in chronological order
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#advanced-studying-vanilla-animations)

Advanced: Studying Vanilla Animations


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To learn more, examine vanilla Hytale animations:

**Path:** `Assets/Common/Blocks/Animations/`

Look at:

*   Door animations
    
*   Chest animations
    
*   Wardrobe animations
    
*   Machine animations
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/06-block-animations#getting-help)

Getting Help


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Discord:** [Official Hytale Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/hytale)
    
*   **Blog:** [Hytale Newsarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news)

# Example Command to Show Title | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [Official Hytale Resourcesarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/)

**Last Modified:** Friday, January 9, 2026 at 12:02 PM

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/11-example-command-show-title#overview)

Overview


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This tutorial demonstrates how to create custom commands that display event titles using Hytale's plugin API. Titles are a powerful way to provide visual feedback to players during events, achievements, or system announcements.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/11-example-command-show-title#example-result)

Example Result


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When executed, the command displays a high-impact title and subtitle directly on the player's screen.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/11-example-command-show-title#command-implementation)

Command Implementation


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/11-example-command-show-title#complete-code-example)

Complete Code Example:

Copy

    public class ModdedCommand extends CommandBase {
        
        public ModdedCommand() {
            // Name, Description, Requires OP
            super("moddedcommand", "A test command", false);
        }
        
        @Override
        protected void executeSync(@Nonnull CommandContext commandContext) {
            // Ensure the sender is a player before proceeding
            commandContext.senderAsPlayer().getWorld().execute(() -> {
                EventTitleUtil.showEventTitleToPlayer(
                    commandContext.senderAsPlayer().getReference(),
                    Message.raw("It's modded!"), // Main Title
                    Message.raw("Yeppers"),      // Subtitle
                    true,                        // Is Major (Shows gold bars/animation)
                    commandContext.senderAsPlayer().getWorld().getEntityStore().getStore()
                );
            });
        }
    }
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/11-example-command-show-title#code-breakdown)

Code Breakdown


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/11-example-command-show-title#id-1.-command-constructor)

1\. Command Constructor

The `super` call defines how players interact with the command in the chat console.

*   `**"moddedcommand"**`: The trigger (e.g., `/moddedcommand`).
    
*   `**"A test command"**`: The tooltip shown in the `/help` menu.
    
*   `**false**`: Setting this to `true` would restrict the command to server operators.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/11-example-command-show-title#id-2.-the-execute-method)

2\. The Execute Method

*   `**executeSync**`: This method runs on the main server thread, making it safe to access world data.
    
*   `**CommandContext**`: Contains data about the `sender`, the `world`, and any `arguments` passed.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/11-example-command-show-title#id-3.-eventtitleutil-parameters)

3\. EventTitleUtil Parameters

The `EventTitleUtil` class handles the packet logic for you:

*   **Player Reference**: Obtained via `senderAsPlayer().getReference()`.
    
*   **Main/Subtitle**: Wrapped in `Message.raw()` to handle plain text.
    
*   **Is Major**: If set to `true`, the title displays with "major" styling (often including decorative bars and a more pronounced animation).
    
*   **Entity Store**: Required for the server to track the display lifecycle relative to the player entity.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/11-example-command-show-title#registering-the-command)

Registering the Command


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To activate your command, register it within the `onEnable()` method of your main plugin class.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/11-example-command-show-title#customization-and-styling)

Customization & Styling


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/11-example-command-show-title#using-colors)

Using Colors

You can use standard Hytale color codes (e.g., `&6` for Gold, `&b` for Aqua) within your messages:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/11-example-command-show-title#formatting-the-duration)

Formatting the Duration

While the basic utility uses default timings, you can also specify fade-in, stay, and fade-out durations using advanced overloads of the `EventTitleUtil` (if available in your API version).

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/11-example-command-show-title#best-practices)

Best Practices


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Thread Safety**: Always wrap world-altering or visual logic in a `world.execute()` block to ensure it runs on the correct synchronization cycle.
    
*   **Player Validation**: Before calling `senderAsPlayer()`, verify the sender is actually a player (and not the console) to avoid `NullPointerExceptions`.
    
*   **Clarity**: Avoid using titles for frequent spam; they are best reserved for significant milestones to maintain their visual impact.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/11-example-command-show-title#getting-help)

Getting Help


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Official Channels:**

*   **Discord:** [Official Hytale Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/hytale)
    
*   **Blog:** [Hytale Newsarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    public class ExamplePlugin extends JavaPlugin {
        
        @Override
        public void onEnable() {
            // Register the command with the server's command manager
            getServer().getCommandManager().registerCommand(new ModdedCommand());
            
            getLogger().info("Modded Title Plugin has been enabled!");
        }
    }

    Message.raw("&6CONGRATULATIONS!")
    Message.raw("&bYou found a secret area.")
