# Useful Tools & Links | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [Official Hytale Resourcesarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/)

**Last Modified:** Friday, January 10, 2026

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This page provides a curated collection of official tools, community resources, and development utilities for Hytale modding. Whether you're creating Packs, developing Plugins, or designing worlds, these resources will help streamline your workflow.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#official-hytale-tools)

Official Hytale Tools


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#blockbench--hytale-plugin)

Blockbench + Hytale Plugin

**Website:** [https://www.blockbench.netarrow-up-right](https://www.blockbench.net/)

**Hytale Plugin:** [https://www.blockbench.net/plugins/hytale\_pluginarrow-up-right](https://www.blockbench.net/plugins/hytale_plugin)

**Plugin Source:** [GitHubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/JannisX11/hytale-blockbench-plugin)

**Official Guide:** [Making Models for Hytalearrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2025/12/an-introduction-to-making-models-for-hytale)

**Description:** The **officially supported** tool for creating Hytale models, textures, and animations. Replaces Hytale's internal modeling tools to support established creative workflows.

**Status:** Releasing soon (Early Access)

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#features)

Features:

*   Create Hytale-compatible models, textures, and animations
    
*   Maintains consistent pixel ratio across textures
    
*   Exports in correct Hytale format
    
*   Quality-of-life improvements for Hytale workflow
    
*   Texture painting and UV mapping
    
*   Real-time preview
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#official-art-style-guidelines)

Official Art Style Guidelines:

*   **Primitives:** Only cubes and quads (no spheres!)
    
*   **Texture Density:** 64px/unit for characters, 32px/unit for props/blocks
    
*   **Texture Size:** Multiples of 32px (32, 64, 96, 128, etc.)
    
*   **Stretching Limits:** 0.7X to 1.3X on any axis
    
*   **Colors:** Avoid pure white and pure black
    
*   **Triangle Count:** Keep optimized for performance
    

**Official Models:** [Download Examplesarrow-up-right](https://cdn.hytale.com/Hytale%20Model%20Examples.zip)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#hytale-asset-editor)

Hytale Asset Editor

**Access:** Built into Hytale (Creation Tools tab)

**Official Info:** [Modding Strategyarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2025/11/hytale-modding-strategy-and-status)

**Description:** Visual editor for data assets (JSON files). Supports most asset types with some limitations.

**Status:** Available now in Early Access

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#features-1)

Features:

*   Edit data assets visually (no coding required)
    
*   Supports blocks, items, and most asset types
    
*   Direct integration with Hytale
    
*   Live preview of changes
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#asset-graph-editor-node-editor)

Asset Graph Editor (Node Editor)

**Access:** Built into Hytale (after launch)

**Official Info:** [World Generation Blogarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2026/1/the-future-of-world-generation)

**Description:** Node-based editor for complex assets like world generation, NPCs, and creative tool brushes.

**Status:** Currently being released

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#features-2)

Features:

*   Visual node-graph interface
    
*   Live-reload in-game
    
*   Build advanced procedural content by linking simple nodes
    
*   Full control over biomes, terrain, props, and materials
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#creative-mode-tools)

Creative Mode Tools

**Access:** Built into Hytale (Creative Mode)

**Official Info:** [Creative Mode Blogarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2025/11/hytale-creative-mode)

**Description:** Interactive suite of in-game tools for world editing and content creation.

**Status:** Available in Early Access

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#tools-available)

Tools Available:

*   **Scripted Brushes:** Asset-defined brushes (mountains, paths, ruins)
    
*   **Shape Brush:** Paint pyramids, cones, squares, and more
    
*   **Selection Tool:** 3D selections, copy, paste, move, rotate
    
*   **Paste Tool:** Precise prefab placement
    
*   **Ruler Tool:** Measure distances and mark outlines
    
*   **Machinima Tool:** Camera animation and recording
    
*   **Prefab Browser/Editor:** Browse and edit prefabs
    
*   **Player Model Changer:** Become any NPC model
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#development-tools)

Development Tools


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#intellij-idea)

IntelliJ IDEA

**Website:** [https://www.jetbrains.com/idea/arrow-up-right](https://www.jetbrains.com/idea/)

**Description:** The recommended IDE for Java plugin development.

**Versions:**

*   **Community Edition:** Free, sufficient for Hytale plugin development
    
*   **Ultimate Edition:** Paid, includes additional features
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/10-useful-tools-and-links#java-development-kit-jdk)

Java Development Kit (JDK)

**Required Version:** Java 25

**Download:**

*   **Oracle JDK:** [https://www.oracle.com/java/arrow-up-right](https://www.oracle.com/java/)
    
*   **OpenJDK:** [https://openjdk.org/arrow-up-right](https://openjdk.org/)
    

**Note:** Hytale plugins require Java 25 specifically.

* * *

###

Gradle

# World Generation Modding | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [The Future of World Generationarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2026/1/the-future-of-world-generation)
 **Last Modified:** Friday, January 10, 2026

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#introduction)

Introduction


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Hytale's world generation system is one of the most powerful modding features available. With the V2 world generator and visual node editor, you can create custom biomes, terrain, and procedural content without writing code.

> **Official Statement:** _"Anyone can create content and modify world-gen without knowing how to code, as V2 can be edited directly in our node editor."_ - Dan (World Generation Engineer)

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#world-generator-versions)

World Generator Versions


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#v1-current-exploration-mode)

V1 (Current - Exploration Mode)

*   **Development:** 2016-2020
    
*   **Status:** Available at Early Access launch
    
*   **Purpose:** Prototype generator with many biomes ready
    
*   **Limitations:** Barriers when creating more zones and complex biomes
    
*   **Future:** Will eventually stop generating new chunks
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#v2-future-orbis)

V2 (Future - Orbis)

*   **Development:** Since 2021
    
*   **Status:** Under construction, accessible via Gateways
    
*   **Purpose:** Next-generation world generator
    
*   **Features:** Addresses V1 limitations, enables global design goals
    
*   **Release:** Will replace V1 once Orbis is complete
    
*   **Compatibility:** Old V1 worlds remain accessible
    

> **Note:** V2 content is currently accessible through Gateways in Exploration mode, allowing early testing.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#key-features-of-v2)

Key Features of V2


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#id-1.-pattern-scanning-system)

1\. Pattern Scanning System

The pattern scanning system allows precise control over prop placement based on environmental context.

**How It Works:**

*   Configure patterns that determine where props are placed
    
*   Search for specific block configurations (e.g., floor = empty block with solid below)
    
*   Add additional checks to gather more environmental context
    
*   Patterns are fully defined by creators
    

**Example Use Cases:**

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#cave-markers)

Cave Markers

*   **Dark ash trees** spawn only above caves in the deeproot biome
    
*   Pattern searches for empty blocks beneath the ground
    
*   Players learn that deeproot caves (with special resources) are found under dark ash trees
    
*   Creates "Heuristics" - deeper patterns that enhance immersion and gameplay
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#log-bridges)

Log Bridges

*   Bridges spawn across rivers by searching for two shores
    
*   Automatically placed where appropriate
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#contextual-vegetation)

Contextual Vegetation

*   Yellow mushrooms and sticks spawn around cedar tree bases
    
*   Glowing mushrooms appear only in sheltered areas
    
*   Meadows of flowers spawn in dips surrounded by trees and boulders
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#id-2.-code-mods-for-programmers)

2\. Code Mods (For Programmers)

**API Features:**

*   Implement mods that automatically work with the node editor
    
*   Plug into vanilla and other modded features
    
*   Simple, interconnected components enable strong capabilities
    
*   Seamless integration between different mods and base game
    

**Technical Benefits:**

*   **Automatic multithreading** - APIs handle threading for you
    
*   **Full read access** - Access to surrounding world context
    
*   **Simplified logic** - Focus on capabilities, not threading
    
*   **Extensibility** - Tweak, extend, and add functionality
    

> **Note:** Detailed technical documentation will be released after launch.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#id-3.-visual-node-editor-no-coding-required)

3\. Visual Node Editor (No Coding Required)

The node editor is the primary tool for creating and modifying world generation.

**Key Features:**

*   **Live-Reload:** World updates in-game as you edit
    
*   **Visual Workflow:** Build advanced procedural content by linking simple nodes
    
*   **No Coding Required:** Accessible with just tutorials and practice
    
*   **Powerful:** Bridges gap between developers and creators
    

**What You Can Control:**

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#terrain-shape)

Terrain Shape

*   Control each biome's terrain shape independently
    
*   High precision control
    
*   Terrain transitions blend features seamlessly between biomes
    
*   Customize terrain at biome edges for better transitions
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#material-providers)

Material Providers

*   Fully control which materials terrain is made of
    
*   Assemble Material Provider nodes with configurable rules
    
*   Access terrain context (block depth, empty space above, etc.)
    
*   Example: Grass material restricted to areas with 10+ blocks of air above
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#props-system)

Props System

*   Generate localized content (POIs, vegetation, decorations)
    
*   Precise control over placement rules and distribution
    
*   Custom procedural point grid
    
*   Customizable rules determine best placement at each point
    
*   Content from prefabs or procedural generation
    

**Editing Workflow:**

*   Each biome is a separate tile (like a jigsaw piece)
    
*   Each zone is its own tile in the world patchwork
    
*   Adding new biomes or content is straightforward
    
*   Same tools used internally by Hytale team
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#official-biomes-available)

Official Biomes Available


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**All Orbis biomes will be shared with the community!**

You'll be able to:

*   View all biomes in the node editor
    
*   Modify existing biomes
    
*   Mix official content with your own creations
    
*   Learn from professional implementations
    

**Regions Shown:**

*   **Emerald Wilds** - Plains-focused biomes
    
*   **Whisperfrost Frontier** - Taiga-focused river biomes
    
*   **Howling Sands** - Desert biomes with oases
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#experimental-feature-packs)

Experimental Feature Packs


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Hytale developers have created experimental terrain packs to showcase possibilities:

*   **Chaotic Stacked Terrain** - Exploring vertical layering
    
*   **Underwater Caves** - Complex cave systems with bracket coral and shipwrecks
    
*   **Arches Terrain** - Natural stone arches theme
    
*   **Floating Islands** - Sky islands theme
    
*   **Procedural Rings** - Alien world with ring systems
    

> **Note:** These are experimental examples, not Adventure mode content.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#modular-asset-structure)

Modular Asset Structure


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Design Philosophy:**

*   Biomes are separate tiles in a zone puzzle
    
*   Zones are tiles in the world patchwork
    
*   Easy to add and edit terrain, props, biomes, and zones
    
*   Same tools creators use as the Hytale team
    

**Benefits:**

*   Straightforward to add new biomes
    
*   Easy to integrate prefabs
    
*   Mix and match content from different sources
    
*   Modular and flexible system
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#future-roadmap)

Future Roadmap


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#short-term-after-launch)

Short-Term (After Launch)

*   Performance improvements
    
*   Upgrading existing features
    
*   More modular and flexible asset structure
    
*   First-party tutorials and guides
    
*   In-depth systems documentation
    
*   Performance optimization best practices
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#long-term)

Long-Term

*   **Procedural Rivers and Paths** - Guide players and connect places
    
*   **Procedural Architecture** - Generate dungeons, ruins, and buildings
    
*   **Organically Growing Fauna** - Increase diversity and coherence
    
*   **Waterfalls** - Dynamic water features
    
*   **Community Feedback Integration** - Shape future based on suggestions
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#world-designer-job-roles)

World Designer Job Roles


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Exciting Opportunity:**

> **Official Announcement:** _"Following the early access release, we plan to expand our team by hiring more than 15 World Designers. These roles will be filled primarily from the community."_ - Simon (CEO)

**What This Means:**

*   New job role that hasn't existed in block games before
    
*   Artists and game designers can apply
    
*   Learn using the same tools Hytale uses internally
    
*   Community members can become professional world designers
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#getting-started-with-world-generation)

Getting Started with World Generation


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#prerequisites)

Prerequisites

*   Understanding of basic Hytale modding concepts
    
*   Familiarity with the Asset Editor
    
*   Creative mindset for procedural design
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#learning-path)

Learning Path

1.  **Explore Existing Biomes** - Study official Orbis biomes in the node editor
    
2.  **Start Simple** - Create basic terrain modifications
    
3.  **Learn Patterns** - Experiment with pattern scanning for props
    
4.  **Build Complexity** - Combine multiple systems
    
5.  **Share and Iterate** - Get community feedback
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#tools-youll-use)

Tools You'll Use

*   **Hytale Node Editor** - Primary world-gen tool
    
*   **Asset Editor** - For asset configuration
    
*   **In-Game Testing** - Live-reload for instant feedback
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#best-practices)

Best Practices


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#design-principles)

Design Principles

*   **Intentional Design** - Curated and procedural balance
    
*   **Heuristics** - Create patterns that enhance immersion
    
*   **Gameplay First** - Design always serves gameplay
    
*   **Resource Balance** - Control resource distribution
    
*   **Breadcrumbing** - Guide players to meaningful content
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#technical-considerations)

Technical Considerations

*   **Performance** - Keep generation efficient
    
*   **Modularity** - Make content easy to modify and extend
    
*   **Compatibility** - Ensure mods work with vanilla and other mods
    
*   **Testing** - Use live-reload for rapid iteration
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#community-support)

Community Support


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#official-resources)

Official Resources

*   **Tutorials** - First-party guides after launch
    
*   **Documentation** - In-depth systems documentation
    
*   **Best Practices** - Performance optimization guides
    
*   **Examples** - All official Orbis biomes available
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#community-channels)

Community Channels

*   **Discord** - [Official Hytale Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/hytale)
    
*   **Feedback** - Community suggestions shape the future
    
*   **Collaboration** - Share techniques and discoveries
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#important-notes)

Important Notes


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#early-access-reality)

Early Access Reality

*   **Asset structure will change frequently** - Core features still being completed
    
*   **Deprecation over removal** - Features being replaced will be deprecated first
    
*   **Active development** - Systems under continuous improvement
    
*   **Support for creators** - Same support given to internal designers
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#compatibility)

Compatibility

*   **V1 Worlds** - Will remain accessible after V2 launch
    
*   **Gateways** - Access V2 content during development
    
*   **Pre-release Testing** - Test Orbis before full release
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#vision-statement)

Vision Statement


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> _"This new approach to world generation will redefine the block-game genre. For the first time, artists and game designers can take full ownership of world generation, with complete control over the final result. This is a fundamental shift away from a world shaped almost solely by programmers."_ - Simon (CEO)

**Goals:**

*   Hytale feels carefully handcrafted while remaining infinitely procedural
    
*   Design always serves gameplay first
    
*   Intentionally expansive - alternate worlds, new dimensions, different spaces
    
*   Beyond Orbis - new blocks, items, prefabs, zones, regions, biomes, NPCs, quests, stories
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/resources-and-tools/16-world-generation-modding#next-steps)

Next Steps


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Wait for Early Access** - V2 tools will be available after launch
    
2.  **Study Official Biomes** - Learn from professional implementations
    
3.  **Join Community** - Connect with other world designers
    
4.  **Experiment** - Try creating simple modifications first
    
5.  **Share Your Work** - Contribute to the ecosystem
    

* * *

Getting Help


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Official Channels:**

*   **Discord:** [Official Hytale Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/hytale)
    
*   **Blog:** [Hytale Newsarrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news)

# Blockbench Modeling Guide | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Source:** [An Introduction to Making Models for Hytalearrow-up-right](https://hytale.com/news/2025/12/an-introduction-to-making-models-for-hytale)
 **Last Modified:** Friday, January 10, 2026

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#introduction)

Introduction


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This guide covers the official Hytale art style and best practices for creating models using Blockbench. Written by Thomas Frick (Art Director), this represents a decade of art direction for Hytale.

> **Note:** _"These are best practices; you don't have to follow them strictly. You are the masters of your own craft, and there is no good or bad way to create as long as you are having fun."_

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#hytale-art-style)

Hytale Art Style


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#definition)

Definition

**"A modern, stylized voxel game, with retro pixel-art textures"**

Hytale's art style combines:

*   Modern game engine capabilities
    
*   Charm of old-school pixel art
    
*   Intersection of low-definition pixel art and hand-painted 3D
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#the-four-art-pillars)

The Four Art Pillars


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Every piece of content in Hytale is evaluated against these core pillars:

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#id-1.-immersive)

1\. Immersive

*   World feels alive, digital nature vanishes
    
*   Motion and detail everywhere
    
*   Wind blows in leaves, creatures wander, clouds travel
    
*   World reacts to the player
    
*   Creatures interact, eyes express emotion
    
*   Lasting impression on players' memories
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#id-2.-fantasy)

2\. Fantasy

*   Deeply fantasy but not limited to medieval
    
*   Art style remains consistent across universes and themes
    
*   Each character has unique personality and twist
    
*   Popular archetypes are reimagined
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#id-3.-stylized)

3\. Stylized

*   Iconic and easily identifiable proportions
    
*   Carefully selected color palette
    
*   Players can read the world regardless of clutter
    
*   **Simplicity is key** - doesn't mean low quality
    
*   Takes many iterations to achieve consistency
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#id-4.-flexible)

4\. Flexible

*   Composed of primitive shapes (cubes and quads)
    
*   Easy to understand how models are made
    
*   Technical structure is simple to comprehend and iterate
    
*   **Empowering user creativity** - true goal of Hytale
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#getting-started)

Getting Started


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#download-required-tools)

Download Required Tools

1.  **Blockbench** - [blockbench.netarrow-up-right](https://www.blockbench.net/)
    
2.  **Hytale Blockbench Plugin** - [Hytale Pluginarrow-up-right](https://www.blockbench.net/plugins/hytale_plugin)
    
3.  **Plugin Source Code** - [GitHubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/JannisX11/hytale-blockbench-plugin)
    

> **Important:** The Blockbench plugin is in Early Access. You might encounter bugs, but it will continue to improve.

**Plugin Features:**

*   Maintains consistent pixel ratio across textures
    
*   Exports models and animations in correct format
    
*   Quality-of-life improvements
    
*   Tailored to Hytale engine needs
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#geometry-constraints)

Geometry Constraints


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#primitives)

Primitives

Hytale models use **only 2 primitives:**

1.  **Cubes** (6 sides)
    
2.  **Quads** (2 sides)
    

**Not Allowed:**

*   ❌ Edge loops
    
*   ❌ Special topology
    
*   ❌ Triangles
    
*   ❌ Pyramids
    
*   ❌ Other traditional modeling shapes
    
*   ❌ **No spheres allowed!**
    

**Benefits:**

*   Easy to make, unwrap, and animate
    
*   No weight painting required
    
*   No rigging required
    
*   No 3D art degree required to start
    
*   Blockbench plugin helps maintain simplicity
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#hytale-proportions)

Hytale Proportions


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#character-bodies)

Character Bodies

*   **Not realistic** - small, bulky, and cartoony
    
*   Supports chunky style used throughout the game
    
*   Blocks and furniture are "toylike"
    
*   Pure and iconic shapes
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#bone-naming-convention)

Bone Naming Convention

*   Bones must be properly named for animation system
    
*   Once bones are correctly named, they animate in-game automatically
    
*   Refer to official player hierarchy for examples
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#triangle-count-polygon-budget)

Triangle Count (Polygon Budget)


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#philosophy)

Philosophy

*   Work as simply as possible
    
*   Increase geometry only when needed to improve silhouette
    
*   Stylistic choice + performance reasons
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#performance-context)

Performance Context

*   Hytale renders **several thousand blocks and voxels simultaneously**
    
*   Results in **several million triangles per frame**
    
*   Triangles are major contributor to FPS loss
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#optimization-requirements)

Optimization Requirements

*   Artists must ensure models are **highly optimized**
    
*   Minimize impact on GPU
    
*   Every triangle counts
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#texture-size-and-density)

Texture Size and Density


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#texture-requirements)

Texture Requirements

*   **Non-square textures allowed**
    
*   Must be **multiples of 32px** (32, 64, 96, 128, etc.)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#texel-density-options)

Texel Density Options

You have **two options** when modeling:

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#option-1-character-attachment)

Option 1: Character/Attachment

*   **Density:** 64px per unit
    
*   **Use For:**
    
    *   Characters
        
    *   Cosmetics
        
    *   Tools
        
    *   Weapons
        
    *   Food items
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#option-2-prop-block)

Option 2: Prop/Block

*   **Density:** 32px per unit
    
*   **Use For:**
    
    *   Cubes
        
    *   Furniture
        
    *   Props
        
    *   Any non-character objects
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#why-higher-density-for-characters)

Why Higher Density for Characters?

**Reasons for 64px density:**

1.  **Emotion Conveyance** - Details on skin, tattoos, makeup, eye/mouth motion
    
2.  **Close-Up Viewing** - Faces seen very close, especially in first-person
    
3.  **Scene Readability** - Characters detach from environment, attract player's eyes
    
4.  **Cosmetic Details** - More options for logos, materials, textures, ornaments
    
5.  **First-Person Immersion** - Hand/weapon/tool looks better close to camera
    

> **Note:** Many avatar customization features will unlock progressively during Early Access.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#stretching-geometry)

Stretching Geometry


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#when-to-use-stretching)

When to Use Stretching

*   Fine adjustments (e.g., avoid Z-fighting when geometry overlaps)
    
*   Slightly resize something
    
*   Work around pixel density limitations
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#stretching-limits)

Stretching Limits

*   **Avoid:** Going under **0.7X** or over **1.3X** stretch on one axis
    
*   Beyond these limits, pixel stretching becomes obvious
    
*   Use sparingly and carefully
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#texturing-brushes)

Texturing Brushes


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#recommended-brushes)

Recommended Brushes

You don't need many special brushes! Use any painting software:

*   Photoshop
    
*   GIMP
    
*   Clip Studio
    
*   Affinity
    
*   Krita
    
*   Blockbench
    
*   Procreate
    

**Two Simple Brushes:**

1.  **Pencil Brush**
    
    *   Opacity on for details
        
    *   Use for color-blocking
        
    
2.  **Round Soft Brush**
    
    *   Opacity pressure on
        
    *   For softening surfaces and creating volume
        
    *   Use for smoothing and shading
        
    
3.  **Opacity Pencil**
    
    *   For polish and final details
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#texturing-philosophy)

Texturing Philosophy

*   Treat each texture as an **"illustration"**
    
*   Paint/bake shadows, ambient occlusion, and highlights directly into texture
    
*   Simulate more complex lighting than exists in-game
    
*   Create illusion of detail
    
*   **Avoid:**
    
    *   Noise
        
    *   Too much grain
        
    *   Perfectly flat surfaces
        
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#color-picking-guidelines)

Color Picking Guidelines


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#color-theory-rules)

Color Theory Rules

**Do:**

*   ✅ Add color in shadows (hint of purple makes models vibrant)
    
*   ✅ Use nuanced, saturated shadows
    
*   ✅ Test colors in-game once available
    

**Don't:**

*   ❌ Use pure white (#FFFFFF)
    
*   ❌ Use pure black (#000000)
    
*   ❌ Create purely desaturated shadows
    

**Why Avoid Pure White/Black:**

*   Breaks lighting in-game
    
*   Adds too much contrast
    
*   Ruins value balance
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#shading-mode-and-materials)

Shading Mode and Materials


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#character-models)

Character Models

*   **Recommendation:** Disable side shadows in Blockbench
    
*   Avoids hard edge effect on body
    
*   Better for simulating curvy organic volumes
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#in-game-materials)

In-Game Materials

*   Tight set of material types (shading modes)
    
*   Performance and style reasons
    
*   Blockbench can't display shading modes yet
    
*   Can set and export shading modes for each node
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#hytale-renderer)

Hytale Renderer


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#rendering-approach)

Rendering Approach

*   **Not using PBR workflows** (no roughness, normal maps, displacement)
    
*   Tailored to elevate unique art style
    
*   Avoids effects that damage handcrafted texture style
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#rendering-features)

Rendering Features

*   Paint lights and shadows inside textures
    
*   Real lights/shadows bring everything together
    
*   In-house light propagation techniques
    
*   Selective shaders and post-processing:
    
    *   Bloom
        
    *   Depth of Field
        
    *   Ambient Occlusion (SSAO)
        
    *   Shadowmap
        
    *   Fog
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#quality-standard)

Quality Standard

*   Models should look good **without any effects**
    
*   Effects are "cherry on top"
    
*   Makes Hytale feel cozy and vibrant
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#future-rendering-features)

Future Rendering Features

*   Light propagation improvements
    
*   Colorimetry and gamma features
    
*   Color grading control
    
*   Godrays
    
*   Transparent glass
    
*   Many other surprises
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#official-tutorial-videos)

Official Tutorial Videos


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Magma Golem Tutorial** by Thomas Frick (Art Director)

*   Concepting process
    
*   Modeling workflow
    
*   Available on official Hytale channels
    

**Download Official Models:**

*   [Hytale Model Examples.ziparrow-up-right](https://cdn.hytale.com/Hytale%20Model%20Examples.zip)
    
*   Includes selection of official models for study and tinkering
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#best-practices-summary)

Best Practices Summary


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#geometry)

Geometry

1.  Use only cubes and quads
    
2.  Keep triangle count low
    
3.  Optimize for performance
    
4.  No spheres!
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#textures)

Textures

1.  Multiples of 32px only
    
2.  Choose correct density (64px for characters, 32px for props)
    
3.  Avoid pure white and pure black
    
4.  Paint shadows and highlights into texture
    
5.  Add color to shadows
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#workflow)

Workflow

1.  Start simple
    
2.  Iterate to improve silhouette
    
3.  Test in-game when possible
    
4.  Follow art pillars (Immersive, Fantasy, Stylized, Flexible)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#character-models-1)

Character Models

1.  Name bones correctly for animation
    
2.  Use 64px density
    
3.  Disable side shadows in Blockbench
    
4.  Keep proportions cartoony and bulky
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#common-mistakes-to-avoid)

Common Mistakes to Avoid


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

❌ **Using too many triangles** - Impacts performance significantly ❌ **Pure white/black colors** - Breaks in-game lighting ❌ **Stretching beyond 0.7X-1.3X** - Obvious pixel distortion ❌ **Wrong texture density** - Inconsistent with game style ❌ **Complex topology** - Keep it simple with cubes and quads ❌ **Flat, noisy textures** - Add volume and avoid grain ❌ **Spheres** - Not supported!

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#learning-resources)

Learning Resources


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#official)

Official

*   **Blockbench Plugin** - Essential tool
    
*   **Model Examples** - Download from official site
    
*   **Tutorial Videos** - Art Director's workflow
    
*   **Official Blog** - Latest art direction updates
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#community)

Community

*   **Discord** - [Official Hytale Discordarrow-up-right](https://discord.gg/hytale)
    
*   **Share Your Work** - Get feedback from community
    
*   **Learn from Others** - Study community creations
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#getting-started-checklist)

Getting Started Checklist


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Download Blockbench
    
*   Install Hytale Blockbench Plugin
    
*   Download official model examples
    
*   Study art pillars
    
*   Practice with simple models
    
*   Choose correct texture density
    
*   Keep geometry simple (cubes and quads only)
    
*   Avoid pure white and black
    
*   Test stretching limits
    
*   Share with community for feedback
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#future-updates)

Future Updates


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Hytale art team will share more about:

*   Advanced modeling techniques
    
*   Animation workflows
    
*   VFX creation
    
*   UI art
    

Stay tuned for more comprehensive guides!

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/packs-content-creation/17-blockbench-modeling-guide#closing-words)

Closing Words


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Plugin Project Template | Hytale Modding Documentation

A minimal, production-ready template for creating Hytale plugins with modern build tools and automated testing.

**GitHub Repository:** [realBritakee/hytale-template-pluginarrow-up-right](https://github.com/realBritakee/hytale-template-plugin)

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Hytale Plugin Template is a ready-to-use project structure that builds immediately without any modifications. It includes modern development tools, automated server testing, and CI/CD workflows to help you start developing plugins quickly.

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#key-features)

Key Features

✅ **Builds Out-of-the-Box** - Clone and run `./gradlew shadowJar` immediately ✅ **Modern Build System** - Gradle 9.2.0 with Kotlin DSL ✅ **Java 25 Support** - Latest Java features ✅ **Automated Server Testing** - Custom Gradle plugin for one-command testing ✅ **ShadowJar Integration** - Automatic dependency bundling ✅ **CI/CD Ready** - GitHub Actions workflow included ✅ **Minimal Structure** - Only essential files, write your own code

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#quick-start)

Quick Start


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#prerequisites)

Prerequisites

*   **Java 25 JDK** - [Download herearrow-up-right](https://www.oracle.com/java/technologies/downloads/)
    
*   **IntelliJ IDEA** - [Download herearrow-up-right](https://www.jetbrains.com/idea/download/)
     (Community Edition works)
    
*   **Git** - [Download herearrow-up-right](https://git-scm.com/)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#id-1.-clone-the-template)

1\. Clone the Template

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#id-2.-build-immediately-no-changes-needed)

2\. Build Immediately (No Changes Needed!)

The template works out-of-the-box:

Your plugin JAR will be in: `build/libs/TemplatePlugin-1.0.0.jar`

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#id-3.-customize-your-plugin)

3\. Customize Your Plugin

When ready to customize, edit these files:

`**settings.gradle.kts**`**:**

`**gradle.properties**`**:**

`**src/main/resources/manifest.json**`**:**

**Rename the main plugin class:**

*   Rename `src/main/java/com/example/templateplugin/TemplatePlugin.java`
    
*   Update package name to match your `pluginGroup`
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#id-4.-implement-your-plugin)

4\. Implement Your Plugin

Write your plugin code in `src/main/java/`:

*   Commands
    
*   Event listeners
    
*   Services
    
*   Storage
    
*   Utilities
    

See [Advanced Plugin Patterns](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns)
 and [Common Plugin Features](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/14-common-plugin-features)
 for examples.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#project-structure)

Project Structure


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Note:** This is a minimal template. Create your own folder structure as needed:

*   `commands/` - For command implementations
    
*   `listeners/` - For event listeners
    
*   `services/` - For business logic
    
*   `storage/` - For data persistence
    
*   `utils/` - For utility classes
    
*   `config/` - For configuration management
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#automated-server-testing)

Automated Server Testing


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The template includes a custom Gradle plugin for automated server testing. This feature is documented in detail in [Gradle Automation & Testing](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/13-gradle-automation-testing)
.

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#quick-usage)

Quick Usage

**Configure in** `**build.gradle.kts**`**:**

**Run the server:**

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#what-it-does)

What It Does

1.  ✅ Downloads the Hytale server JAR (cached for future runs)
    
2.  ✅ Compiles your plugin with `shadowJar`
    
3.  ✅ Copies the plugin to `run/plugins/`
    
4.  ✅ Starts the server with interactive console
    
5.  ✅ Supports debug mode: `./gradlew runServer -Pdebug`
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#features)

Features

*   **Smart Caching** - Downloads server JAR once, reuses forever
    
*   **Auto-Deploy** - Builds and deploys your plugin automatically
    
*   **Interactive Console** - Type commands directly in the terminal
    
*   **Debug Support** - Connect your IDE debugger to port 5005
    
*   **Clean Workspace** - Server files in `run/` directory (gitignored)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#development-workflow)

Development Workflow

Adding Dependencies


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Edit `build.gradle.kts`:

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#dependency-relocation)

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#ci-cd-with-github-actions)

CI/CD with GitHub Actions


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The template includes a GitHub Actions workflow (`.github/workflows/build.yml`) that:

1.  ✅ Builds your plugin on every push
    
2.  ✅ Runs tests
    
3.  ✅ Uploads artifacts
    
4.  ✅ Creates releases when you tag
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#creating-a-release)

Creating a Release

GitHub Actions will automatically build and create a release with your plugin JAR.

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#workflow-features)

Workflow Features

*   **Multi-OS Testing** - Builds on Ubuntu, Windows, and macOS
    
*   **Java 25 Support** - Uses the latest Java version
    
*   **Artifact Upload** - Saves built JARs for download
    
*   **Release Automation** - Automatically creates GitHub releases

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#customization-examples)

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#recommended-folder-structure)

Recommended Folder Structure


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once you start developing, organize your code like this:

See [Advanced Plugin Patterns](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns)
 for implementation details.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#best-practices)

Best Practices


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#do)

✅ DO:

*   Use the Service-Storage pattern for data management
    
*   Write unit tests for your business logic
    
*   Use structured logging (not `System.out.println`)
    
*   Handle errors gracefully with try-catch blocks
    
*   Document your public API with JavaDoc
    
*   Version your releases semantically (1.0.0, 1.1.0, etc.)
    
*   Use dependency injection where possible
    
*   Keep your main class minimal
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#dont)

❌ DON'T:

*   Hardcode configuration values
    
*   Block the main thread with heavy operations
    
*   Ignore exceptions or use empty catch blocks
    
*   Use deprecated APIs
    
*   Commit sensitive data (API keys, passwords)
    
*   Mix business logic with storage logic
    
*   Use static variables for state management
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#build-fails)

Build Fails

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#server-wont-start)

Server Won't Start

1.  Check that `jarUrl` in `build.gradle.kts` is correct
    
2.  Verify Java 25 is installed: `java -version`
    
3.  Check logs in `run/logs/`
    
4.  Ensure the server JAR is compatible
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#plugin-not-loading)

Plugin Not Loading

1.  Verify `manifest.json` has correct `Main` class path
    
2.  Check server logs for errors
    
3.  Ensure all dependencies are bundled in JAR
    
4.  Verify the plugin JAR is in `run/plugins/`
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#gradle-daemon-issues)

Gradle Daemon Issues

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/15-plugin-project-template#migration-from-other-templates)

Migration from Other Templates


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you're migrating from another template:

1.  **Copy your source code** to `src/main/java/`
    
2.  **Update** `**manifest.json**` with your plugin metadata
    
3.  **Copy dependencies** to `build.gradle.kts`
    
4.  **Update package names** to match your group
    
5.  **Test the build** with `./gradlew shadowJar`
    

* * *

Copy

    git clone https://github.com/realBritakee/hytale-template-plugin.git
    cd hytale-template-plugin

Copy

    # Windows
    gradlew.bat shadowJar
    
    # Linux/Mac
    ./gradlew shadowJar

Copy

    rootProject.name = "your-plugin-name"

Copy

    pluginGroup=com.yourname
    pluginVersion=1.0.0
    pluginDescription=Your plugin description

Copy

    {
      "Group": "YourName",
      "Name": "YourPluginName",
      "Main": "com.yourname.yourplugin.YourPlugin"
    }

Copy

    hytale-template-plugin/
    ├── .github/workflows/
    │   └── build.yml                    # CI/CD workflow
    ├── buildSrc/
    │   ├── build.gradle.kts             # Custom plugin configuration
    │   └── src/main/kotlin/
    │       └── RunHytalePlugin.kt       # Automated server testing
    ├── gradle/wrapper/
    │   ├── gradle-wrapper.jar           # Gradle wrapper binary
    │   └── gradle-wrapper.properties    # Gradle 9.2.0 configuration
    ├── src/main/
    │   ├── java/com/example/templateplugin/
    │   │   └── TemplatePlugin.java      # Minimal main class (example)
    │   └── resources/
    │       ├── manifest.json            # Plugin metadata
    │       └── config.json              # Example configuration
    ├── .gitignore                       # Git ignore rules
    ├── build.gradle.kts                 # Build configuration
    ├── gradle.properties                # Project properties
    ├── gradlew                          # Gradle wrapper (Unix)
    ├── gradlew.bat                      # Gradle wrapper (Windows)
    ├── settings.gradle.kts              # Project settings
    ├── LICENSE                          # MIT License
    └── README.md                        # Documentation

Copy

    runHytale {
        jarUrl = "url to hytale server jar"
    }

Copy

    # Windows
    gradlew.bat runServer
    
    # Linux/Mac
    ./gradlew runServer

Copy

    # Compile only
    ./gradlew compileJava
    
    # Build plugin JAR
    ./gradlew shadowJar
    
    # Clean and rebuild
    ./gradlew clean shadowJar

Copy

    # Run server with your plugin
    ./gradlew runServer
    
    # Run unit tests
    ./gradlew test
    
    # Clean test server
    rm -rf run/

Copy

    # Run server in debug mode
    ./gradlew runServer -Pdebug
    
    # Then connect your IDE debugger to localhost:5005

Copy

    dependencies {
        // Hytale API (provided by server)
        compileOnly(files("libs/hytale-server.jar"))
        
        // Your dependencies (will be bundled)
        implementation("com.google.code.gson:gson:2.10.1")
        implementation("org.jetbrains:annotations:24.1.0")
        
        // Test dependencies
        testImplementation("org.junit.jupiter:junit-jupiter:5.10.0")
        testRuntimeOnly("org.junit.platform:junit-platform-launcher")
    }

Copy

    tasks {
        shadowJar {
            // Relocate dependencies to avoid conflicts
            relocate("com.google.gson", "com.yourplugin.libs.gson")
            relocate("org.apache.commons", "com.yourplugin.libs.commons")
            
            // Minimize JAR size (removes unused classes)
            minimize()
        }
    }

Copy

    git tag v1.0.0
    git push origin v1.0.0

Copy

    java {
        toolchain {
            languageVersion.set(JavaLanguageVersion.of(21))
        }
    }
    
    tasks {
        compileJava {
            options.release = 21
        }
    }

Copy

    repositories {
        mavenLocal()
        mavenCentral()
        maven("https://repo.example.com/releases")
    }

Copy

    tasks.register("copyToServer") {
        group = "deployment"
        description = "Copy plugin to local server"
        
        doLast {
            val serverDir = File("C:/HytaleServer/plugins")
            val pluginJar = tasks.shadowJar.get().outputs.files.singleFile
            pluginJar.copyTo(File(serverDir, pluginJar.name), overwrite = true)
            println("Plugin copied to server!")
        }
    }

Copy

    src/main/java/com/yourname/yourplugin/
    ├── YourPlugin.java              # Main class
    ├── commands/
    │   ├── CommandManager.java      # Command registration
    │   ├── HelpCommand.java
    │   └── ReloadCommand.java
    ├── listeners/
    │   ├── PlayerJoinListener.java
    │   └── BlockBreakListener.java
    ├── services/
    │   ├── PlayerService.java       # Business logic
    │   └── DataService.java
    ├── storage/
    │   ├── PlayerStorage.java       # Data persistence
    │   └── ConfigStorage.java
    ├── config/
    │   ├── PluginConfig.java        # Configuration classes
    │   └── Messages.java
    └── utils/
        ├── TextUtils.java           # Utility methods
        └── TimeUtils.java

Copy

    # Clean and rebuild
    ./gradlew clean build --refresh-dependencies
    
    # Check Gradle version
    ./gradlew --version
    
    # Update Gradle wrapper
    ./gradlew wrapper --gradle-version=9.2.0

Copy

    # Stop all Gradle daemons
    ./gradlew --stop
    
    # Rebuild
    ./gradlew clean shadowJar

# Advanced Plugin Patterns | Hytale Modding Documentation

**Last Modified:** Friday, January 10, 2026

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This guide covers advanced architectural patterns and best practices for building robust, scalable Hytale plugins. These patterns are commonly used in production plugins and will help you write cleaner, more maintainable code.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#plugin-architecture-patterns)

Plugin Architecture Patterns


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#service-storage-pattern)

Service-Storage Pattern

A common pattern for managing data in plugins is to separate **business logic** (Service) from **data persistence** (Storage).

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#benefits)

Benefits:

*   Clean separation of concerns
    
*   Easy to swap storage backends (JSON → Database)
    
*   Testable business logic
    
*   In-memory caching layer
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#example-structure)

Example Structure:

Copy

    // Storage Interface - Handles data persistence
    public interface PlayerStorage {
        PlayerData load(UUID uuid);
        void save(PlayerData data);
        List<PlayerData> loadAll();
    }
    
    // JSON Implementation
    public class PlayerJsonStorage implements PlayerStorage {
        private final File dataFolder;
        
        public PlayerJsonStorage(File dataFolder) {
            this.dataFolder = new File(dataFolder, "players");
            this.dataFolder.mkdirs();
        }
        
        @Override
        public PlayerData load(UUID uuid) {
            File file = new File(dataFolder, uuid.toString() + ".json");
            if (!file.exists()) return null;
            
            try (FileReader reader = new FileReader(file)) {
                return new Gson().fromJson(reader, PlayerData.class);
            } catch (IOException e) {
                e.printStackTrace();
                return null;
            }
        }
        
        @Override
        public void save(PlayerData data) {
            File file = new File(dataFolder, data.getUuid().toString() + ".json");
            
            try (FileWriter writer = new FileWriter(file)) {
                new Gson().toJson(data, writer);
            } catch (IOException e) {
                e.printStackTrace();
            }
        }
        
        @Override
        public List<PlayerData> loadAll() {
            List<PlayerData> players = new ArrayList<>();
            File[] files = dataFolder.listFiles((dir, name) -> name.endsWith(".json"));
            
            if (files != null) {
                for (File file : files) {
                    try (FileReader reader = new FileReader(file)) {
                        players.add(new Gson().fromJson(reader, PlayerData.class));
                    } catch (IOException e) {
                        e.printStackTrace();
                    }
                }
            }
            
            return players;
        }
    }
    
    // Service Layer - Business logic and caching
    public class PlayerService {
        private final PlayerStorage storage;
        private final Map<UUID, PlayerData> cache;
        
        public PlayerService(PlayerStorage storage) {
            this.storage = storage;
            this.cache = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
            loadAll();
        }
        
        private void loadAll() {
            for (PlayerData data : storage.loadAll()) {
                cache.put(data.getUuid(), data);
            }
        }
        
        public PlayerData getPlayer(UUID uuid) {
            return cache.computeIfAbsent(uuid, id -> {
                PlayerData data = storage.load(id);
                return data != null ? data : new PlayerData(id);
            });
        }
        
        public void savePlayer(PlayerData data) {
            cache.put(data.getUuid(), data);
            storage.save(data);
        }
        
        public void saveAll() {
            for (PlayerData data : cache.values()) {
                storage.save(data);
            }
        }
    }

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#thread-pool-management)

Thread Pool Management


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For async operations, use a thread pool instead of creating new threads repeatedly.

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#why-use-thread-pools)

Why Use Thread Pools?

*   **Performance**: Reuses threads instead of creating new ones
    
*   **Resource Management**: Limits concurrent threads
    
*   **Scheduled Tasks**: Built-in support for delayed/periodic tasks
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#implementation)

Implementation:

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#singleton-pattern-for-plugin-access)

Singleton Pattern for Plugin Access


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Allow other parts of your code (and other plugins) to access your plugin instance.

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#implementation-1)

Implementation:

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#logging-best-practices)

Logging Best Practices


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#structured-logging-with-log-levels)

Configuration Management


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#type-safe-configuration)

Type-Safe Configuration

Instead of accessing config values directly everywhere, create a configuration class:

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#event-system-pattern)

Event System Pattern


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create a custom event system for your plugin to allow extensibility.

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#basic-event-system)

Basic Event System:

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#periodic-save-pattern)

Periodic Save Pattern


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Automatically save data at regular intervals to prevent data loss.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#cache-cleanup-pattern)

Cache Cleanup Pattern


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Periodically clean up unused cached data to prevent memory leaks.

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#plugin-lifecycle-best-practices)

Plugin Lifecycle Best Practices


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#complete-plugin-template-with-all-patterns)

Complete Plugin Template with All Patterns:

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#summary)

Summary


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#key-patterns-covered)

Key Patterns Covered:

1.  **Service-Storage Pattern** - Separate business logic from data persistence
    
2.  **Thread Pool Management** - Efficient async operations
    
3.  **Singleton Pattern** - Global plugin access
    
4.  **Structured Logging** - Professional logging with levels and files
    
5.  **Type-Safe Configuration** - Clean config management
    
6.  **Custom Event System** - Extensible plugin architecture
    
7.  **Periodic Save Pattern** - Automatic data persistence
    
8.  **Cache Cleanup Pattern** - Memory management
    

### 

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#benefits-1)

Benefits:

*   **Maintainable**: Clear separation of concerns
    
*   **Scalable**: Easy to add new features
    
*   **Testable**: Services can be tested independently
    
*   **Professional**: Production-ready patterns
    
*   **Extensible**: Other plugins can integrate via your API
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#next-steps)

Next Steps


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Implement these patterns in your plugin
    
*   Create unit tests for your services
    
*   Document your public API
    
*   Consider creating a developer API for other plugins
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://britakee-studios.gitbook.io/hytale-modding-documentation/plugins-java-development/12-advanced-plugin-patterns#getting-help)
